a television selection service being used, or being used in a manner specified
in the regulations, by no fewer than such number of members of the public in
the United Kingdom as may be specified in the regulations;

28.1.362AF.3.b

the date on which a television selection service is first made available to
members of the public in the United Kingdom;

28.1.362AF.3.c

the functions that a television selection service is capable of carrying out
or may be made capable of carrying out.

28.1.362AF.4

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) (a)  or  (b) , the Secretary
of State must have received a report under  section 362AG  relating to the
television selection service or description of television selection services
in question.

############ Advice from OFCOM

28.1.362AG

28.1.362AG.1

OFCOM may prepare reports making recommendations about the exercise of the
power under  section 362AF (1) (a)  or  (b) .

28.1.362AG.2

Where—

28.1.362AG.2.a

the Secretary of State proposes to make regulations under  section 362AF (1)
(a)  or  (b) , and

28.1.362AG.2.b

the Secretary of State has not received a report under  subsection (1)
relating to the television selection service or description of television
selection services that would be affected by the proposed regulations,

the Secretary of State must request OFCOM to prepare a report making
recommendations about the exercise of the power under  section 362AF (1) (a)
or  (b)  in relation to that service or services of that description.

28.1.362AG.3

Where the Secretary of State makes a request under  subsection (2) , OFCOM
must prepare such a report as soon as practicable.

28.1.362AG.4

A report under  subsection (1)  or  (3)  relating to the exercise of the power
under  section 362AF (1) (a)  must include OFCOM’s assessment of—

28.1.362AG.4.a

the number of members of the public in the United Kingdom using that service
and whether that number is significant;

28.1.362AG.4.b

the manner in which that service is used by such persons;

28.1.362AG.4.c

whether that service is capable of functioning as a regulated television
selection service and the modifications, if any, that are needed to make it so
capable;

28.1.362AG.4.d

such matters as OFCOM consider likely to affect the matters referred to in
paragraphs  (a)  to  (c) .

28.1.362AG.5

A report under  subsection (1)  or  (3)  relating to the exercise of the power
under  section 362AF (1) (b)  must include OFCOM’s assessment of—

28.1.362AG.5.a

which television selection services are likely to fall within the description
of television selection services in question;

28.1.362AG.5.b

such matters as OFCOM consider relevant to the assessment described in
paragraph  (a) .

28.1.362AG.6

OFCOM must give the Secretary of State a report prepared under  subsection (1)
or  (3) .

28.1.362AG.7

If the Secretary of State exercises the power under  section 362AF (1) (a)  or
(b)  in a manner which differs materially from recommendations made in a
report under this section, the Secretary of State must publish, no later than
the time at which the regulations are made, a statement giving the Secretary
of State’s reasons for doing so.

28.1.362AG.8

OFCOM must publish reports given to the Secretary of State under this section.

28.1.362AG.9

OFCOM must prepare and publish a statement about the principles and methods
applied by OFCOM in preparing a report under  subsection (1)  or  (3) .

28.1.362AG.10

OFCOM may revise or replace a statement published under this section and,
where they do so, must publish the revised or replacement statement.

########### Notification by providers of television selection services

############ Notification by providers of television selection services

28.1.362AH

28.1.362AH.1

A provider of a television selection service must give notice to OFCOM if the
service is or becomes a television selection service of a description
specified in regulations made by virtue of  section 362AF (1) (b) .

28.1.362AH.2

A provider of a television selection service must give notice to OFCOM if,
having been a service of a description specified in regulations made by virtue
of  section 362AF (1) (b) , the service ceases to be a service of such a
description.

28.1.362AH.3

A provider of a regulated television selection service must give notice to
OFCOM if the provider ceases to provide that service.

28.1.362AH.4

A notice given to OFCOM under this section must—

28.1.362AH.4.a

be sent in such manner as OFCOM may require;

28.1.362AH.4.b

contain such information as OFCOM may require.

########### Lists of services

############ Lists of services

28.1.362AI

28.1.362AI.1

OFCOM must establish and maintain up to date lists of—

28.1.362AI.1.a

designated internet programme services; and

28.1.362AI.1.b

regulated television selection services and their providers.

28.1.362AI.2

OFCOM must publish the up to date lists on a publicly accessible part of their
website.

########### Must-offer and must-carry obligations

############ Must-offer obligations in the case of designated internet programme services

28.1.362AJ

28.1.362AJ.1

The provider of a designated internet programme service must at all times
offer the service as available (subject to the need to agree terms) to be, in
relation to every regulated television selection service, included in the
regulated television selection service.

28.1.362AJ.2

The provider of a designated internet programme service must do its best to
secure that, in relation to every regulated television selection service,
arrangements are entered into, and kept in force, that ensure that the service
is included in the regulated television selection service.

28.1.362AJ.3

The provider of a designated internet programme service must act consistently
with the agreement objectives when entering into such arrangements and while
they are in force.

28.1.362AJ.4

Subsections  (1)  to  (3)  do not apply where the provider of a designated
internet programme service is the BBC.

############ Must-carry obligations

28.1.362AK

28.1.362AK.1

The provider of a regulated television selection service must—

28.1.362AK.1.a

in respect of each designated internet programme service, enter into
arrangements with the provider of the designated internet programme service
for the regulated television selection service to include that designated
internet programme service, and

28.1.362AK.1.b

keep them in force.

28.1.362AK.2

The provider of a regulated television selection service must act consistently
with the agreement objectives when entering into arrangements in pursuance of
subsection (1)  and while they are in force.

28.1.362AK.3

For provision applying where there is a dispute about the arrangements that
should be made or their operation, see sections  362AT  to  362AY .

############ Guidance as regards agreement objectives

28.1.362AL

28.1.362AL.1

OFCOM must prepare and publish guidance about how providers of designated
internet programme services and providers of regulated television selection
services may act consistently with the agreement objectives.

28.1.362AL.2

The reference in  subsection (1)  to acting consistently with the agreement
objectives is to be treated, in relation to the BBC, as a reference to
carrying out any duty of the BBC under the BBC Charter and Agreement that is
comparable to the duty of providers of designated internet programme services
other than the BBC under  section 362AJ (3) .

28.1.362AL.3

OFCOM may revise and replace any guidance published under this section and,
where they do, must publish the revised or replacement guidance.

28.1.362AL.4

Before preparing guidance under this section (or revising or replacing it),
OFCOM must consult—

28.1.362AL.4.a

the Secretary of State, and

28.1.362AL.4.b

such other persons as they consider appropriate.

28.1.362AL.5

In exercising or deciding whether to exercise any of their powers under
sections  362AU  to  362AX , OFCOM must have regard to any guidance for the
time being published under this section.

############ Meaning of “the agreement objectives”

28.1.362AM

28.1.362AM.1

In sections  362AJ  to  362AL  “the agreement objectives” are—

28.1.362AM.1.a

that a designated internet programme service is given an appropriate degree of
prominence within a regulated television selection service;

28.1.362AM.1.b

that, in a case where a designated internet programme service contributes to—

28.1.362AM.1.b.i

the fulfilment of the public service remit for a licensed public service
channel,

28.1.362AM.1.b.ii

the fulfilment of S4C’s public service remit, or

28.1.362AM.1.b.iii

the promotion of one or more of the BBC’s public purposes,

the arrangements made between the provider of that designated internet
programme service and the provider of a regulated television selection service
do not adversely affect the ability of the provider of that channel to fulfil
the public service remit for that channel, the ability of S4C to fulfil S4C’s
public service remit or (as the case may be) the ability of the BBC to promote
its public purposes;

28.1.362AM.1.c

that arrangements so made do not disproportionately restrict how the provider
of a regulated television selection service may make innovations in the ways
that users may select and access internet programme services or programmes
included in such services.

28.1.362AM.2

The reference in  subsection (1) (a)  to a designated internet programme
service being given an appropriate degree of prominence within a regulated
television selection service includes a reference to an appropriate degree of
prominence being given to public service remit content and any listed channel
included in that designated internet programme service, so far as the
prominence of that content or channel is capable of being affected by the
operation of the regulated television selection service.

28.1.362AM.3

The following are listed channels for the purposes of this section—

28.1.362AM.3.a

any service of television programmes provided by the BBC so as to be available
for use by members of the public;

28.1.362AM.3.b

any Channel 3 service;

28.1.362AM.3.c

Channel 4;

28.1.362AM.3.d

Channel 5;

28.1.362AM.3.e

S4C Digital.

########### Duties relating to a designated internet programme service

############ Duties relating to a designated internet programme service

28.1.362AN

28.1.362AN.1

The provider of a designated internet programme service must ensure that—

28.1.362AN.1.a

the service makes such contribution as is described in  subsection (3) (a) ,
subsection (4) (a)  or (as the case may be)  subsection (5) (a)  of  section
362AA , and

28.1.362AN.1.b

such material included in the service as is described in  subsection (3) (b) ,
subsection (4) (b)  or (as the case may be)  subsection (5) (b)  of  section
362AA  is readily discoverable and is promoted by the service.

28.1.362AN.2

Subsection (1)  does not apply where the provider of a designated internet
programme service is the BBC.

########### Duties relating to a regulated television selection service

############ Duties relating to a regulated television selection service

28.1.362AO

28.1.362AO.1

A provider of a regulated television selection service must secure that the
manner in which its service presents internet programme services to its users
in the United Kingdom gives an appropriate degree of prominence to each of the
designated internet programme services included in its service.

28.1.362AO.2

Subsection  (1)  does not require that a designated internet programme service
be given prominence, or the same degree of prominence, in relation to every
area of the United Kingdom.

28.1.362AO.3

The reference in subsection  (1)  to giving an appropriate degree of
prominence to a designated internet programme service included in a regulated
television selection service includes a reference to giving an appropriate
degree of prominence to—

28.1.362AO.3.a

material that is public service remit content or contributes to the promotion
of one or more of the BBC’s public purposes included in that designated
internet programme service, and

28.1.362AO.3.b

any listed channel included in that designated internet programme service,

so far as the prominence of that material or channel is affected by the
operation of the regulated television selection service.

28.1.362AO.4

A provider of a regulated television selection service must incorporate
features in the service that secure that persons with disabilities, in
particular those affecting their sight or hearing or both—

28.1.362AO.4.a

are able, so far as practicable, to make use of the service for all the same
purposes as persons without disabilities; and

28.1.362AO.4.b

are informed about, and are able to make use of, whatever assistance for
disabled people is provided in relation to the internet programme services
included in the service.

28.1.362AO.5

In this section “ assistance for disabled people ” has the same meaning as in
Part 3 (see section 362(1)).

############ Code of practice

28.1.362AP

28.1.362AP.1

OFCOM must issue a code of practice describing actions that OFCOM recommend
for the purpose of securing that the manner in which a regulated television
selection service presents internet programme services to its users complies
with the duties in  section 362AO .

28.1.362AP.2

OFCOM may—

28.1.362AP.2.a

revise a code of practice issued under this section and issue the code as
revised;

28.1.362AP.2.b

withdraw a code of practice issued under this section and issue a new code of
practice.

28.1.362AP.3

OFCOM must—

28.1.362AP.3.a

publish a code of practice issued under this section in such manner as they
consider appropriate;

28.1.362AP.3.b

keep a code of practice issued under this section under review.

28.1.362AP.4

If requested by the Secretary of State to review all or part of a code of
practice issued under this section, OFCOM must review the code or that part of
it.

28.1.362AP.5

OFCOM must secure that the actions recommended in a code of practice issued
under this section are consistent with the agreement objectives.

28.1.362AP.6

The actions recommended in a code of practice issued under this section may
include—

28.1.362AP.6.a

actions relating to particular descriptions of regulated television selection
services;

28.1.362AP.6.b

actions relating to particular descriptions of internet programme services.

############ Effects of the code of practice

28.1.362AQ

28.1.362AQ.1

The provider of a regulated television selection service is to be treated as
complying with the duty in  section 362AO (1)  or  (4)  if the provider takes
the actions described in the code of practice which are recommended for the
purpose of complying with the duty.

28.1.362AQ.2

A failure by the provider of a regulated television selection service to act
in accordance with a provision of the code of practice does not of itself make
the provider liable to legal proceedings before a court or tribunal.

28.1.362AQ.3

In any legal proceedings before a court or tribunal, the court or tribunal
must take into account a provision of the code of practice in determining any
question arising in the proceedings if—

28.1.362AQ.3.a

the question relates to a time when the provision was in force, and

28.1.362AQ.3.b

the provision appears to the court or tribunal to be relevant to the question.

28.1.362AQ.4

OFCOM must take into account a provision of the code of practice in
determining any question arising in connection with the carrying out by them
of a relevant function if—

28.1.362AQ.4.a

the question relates to a time when the provision was in force, and

28.1.362AQ.4.b

the provision appears to OFCOM to be relevant to the question.

28.1.362AQ.5

In this section, “ relevant function ” means a function conferred on OFCOM by
any of the following provisions—

28.1.362AQ.5.a

sections  362AT  to  362AY  (references of disputes to OFCOM), and

28.1.362AQ.5.b

sections  362AZ  to  362AZ5  (enforcement).

############ Issuing a code of practice

28.1.362AR

28.1.362AR.1

Before issuing a code of practice under  section 362AP , OFCOM—

28.1.362AR.1.a

must publish a draft of the code or (as the case may be) a draft of the
revisions of the existing code;

28.1.362AR.1.b

must consult the following about the draft—

28.1.362AR.1.b.i

the Secretary of State;

28.1.362AR.1.b.ii

public service broadcasters;

28.1.362AR.1.b.iii

such persons who appear to OFCOM to represent providers of regulated
television selection services;

28.1.362AR.1.b.iv

such other persons as OFCOM consider appropriate;

28.1.362AR.1.c

may make such alterations to the draft as OFCOM consider appropriate following
the consultation.

28.1.362AR.2

Subsection  (1)  does not apply in relation to revisions of the code of
practice if—

28.1.362AR.2.a

OFCOM give the Secretary of State a draft of the revisions of the existing
code, and

28.1.362AR.2.b

the Secretary of State agrees that it is not necessary for  subsection (1)  to
apply in relation to the revisions.

########### Power to require information

############ Power to require information

28.1.362AS

28.1.362AS.1

OFCOM may by notice (an “information notice”) require a person within
subsection (4)  to provide them with any information that they require for the
purpose of carrying out their functions under this Part.

28.1.362AS.2

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  includes power to require a person
within  subsection (4)  to obtain or generate information.

28.1.362AS.3

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  must be exercised in a way that is
proportionate to the use to which the information is to be put by OFCOM.

28.1.362AS.4

The persons within this subsection are—

28.1.362AS.4.a

a public service broadcaster;

28.1.362AS.4.b

a provider of an internet programme service;

28.1.362AS.4.c

a provider of a television selection service;

28.1.362AS.4.d

a person who provides an ancillary service in relation to an internet
programme service or a television selection service;

28.1.362AS.4.e

a manufacturer of apparatus that is, or in combination with other apparatus
is, internet television equipment;

28.1.362AS.4.f

a person who creates or provides software used in association with such
apparatus;

28.1.362AS.4.g

a person who was within any of paragraphs  (a)  to  (f)  at a time to which
the required information relates;

28.1.362AS.4.h

a person who is not within any of paragraphs  (a)  to  (g)  but who appears to
OFCOM to have, or to be able to obtain or generate, information required by
them as mentioned in  subsection (1) .

28.1.362AS.5

The information that OFCOM may require under  subsection (1)  includes, in
particular, information that they require for any one or more of the following
purposes—

28.1.362AS.5.a

the purpose of deciding whether to designate an internet programme service for
the purposes of this Part or to revoke such a designation;

28.1.362AS.5.b

the purpose of assessing compliance with  section 362AD (1)  (duty to notify
OFCOM where cease to be associated with a public service broadcaster);

28.1.362AS.5.c

the purpose of preparing a report under  section 362AG  (advice from OFCOM
about the designation of television selection services etc);

28.1.362AS.5.d

the purpose of assessing compliance with  section 362AH  (duty of providers of
television selection services to notify OFCOM);

28.1.362AS.5.e

the purpose of assessing compliance with any duty of a provider of a
designated internet programme service under  section 362AJ  or  362AN  (must-
offer and content of designated internet programme services obligations);

28.1.362AS.5.f

the purpose of assessing compliance with any duty of the BBC under the BBC
Charter and Agreement that is comparable to any duty of a provider of a
designated internet programme service under  section 362AJ  or  362AN ;

28.1.362AS.5.g

the purpose of assessing compliance with any duty of a provider of a regulated
television selection service under  section 362AK  or  362AO  (must-carry and
prominence obligations);

28.1.362AS.5.h

the purpose of preparing or reviewing a code of practice under  section 362AP
(code of practice relating to duties under  section 362AO );

28.1.362AS.5.i

the purpose of OFCOM’s functions under sections  362AT  to  362AY  (dispute
resolution);

28.1.362AS.5.j

the purpose of assessing compliance with any requirements imposed by a
confirmation decision under  section 362AZ1 ;

28.1.362AS.5.k

the purpose of determining the appropriate fee that a provider is required to
pay under  section 362AZ6 ;

28.1.362AS.5.l

the purpose of OFCOM’s monitoring role under  section 362AZ9 ;

28.1.362AS.5.m

the purpose of ascertaining the amount of a person’s or a group of entities’
qualifying worldwide revenue for the purposes of  paragraph 3  or  4  of
Schedule 16A .

28.1.362AS.6

An information notice must—

28.1.362AS.6.a

specify or describe the information to be provided,

28.1.362AS.6.b

specify why OFCOM require the information,

28.1.362AS.6.c

specify the form and manner in which the information must be provided, and

28.1.362AS.6.d

contain information about the consequences of not complying with the notice.

28.1.362AS.7

An information notice must specify when the information must be provided which
may be—

28.1.362AS.7.a

on or by a specified date, or

28.1.362AS.7.b

within a specified period.

28.1.362AS.8

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  does not include power to require the
provision of information in respect of which a claim to legal professional
privilege, or (in Scotland) to confidentiality of communications, could be
maintained in legal proceedings.

28.1.362AS.9

A person to whom an information notice is given must provide the information
in accordance with any requirements included in the notice (subject to
subsection (10) ).

28.1.362AS.10

The duty under  subsection (9)  does not require a disclosure of information
if that disclosure would contravene the data protection legislation (but, in
determining whether a disclosure would do so, that duty is to be taken into
account).

28.1.362AS.11

For the purposes of  subsection (4) (d) , a service is an “ ancillary service
” in relation to an internet programme service or a television selection
service if it facilitates the provision of that service (or part of it),
whether directly or indirectly.

28.1.362AS.12

In this section, a reference to the functions of OFCOM under this Part
includes a reference to their functions under  Schedules 16A  and  16B , so
far as relating to this Part.

28.1.362AS.13

In this section, “ data protection legislation ” has the same meaning as in
the Data Protection Act 2018 (see section 3 of that Act).

########### References of disputes to OFCOM

############ References of disputes to OFCOM

28.1.362AT

28.1.362AT.1

This section applies in the case of a dispute between the provider of a
designated internet programme service and the provider of a regulated
television selection service about—

28.1.362AT.1.a

the arrangements that should be made between them in order to give effect to
the prominence duties that relate to them, or

28.1.362AT.1.b

the operation of arrangements made between them in order to give effect to
those duties.

28.1.362AT.2

For the purposes of  subsection (1) —

28.1.362AT.2.a

the prominence duties relating to the provider of a designated internet
programme service are—

28.1.362AT.2.a.i

in the case of a provider other than the BBC, the duties under  section 362AJ
;

28.1.362AT.2.a.ii

in the case of the BBC, any duties of the BBC under the BBC Charter and
Agreement that are comparable to the duties of other providers under  section
362AJ ;

28.1.362AT.2.b

the prominence duties relating to the provider of a regulated television
selection service are the duties under sections  362AK  and  362AO (1) .

28.1.362AT.3

Any one or more of the parties to the dispute may refer it to OFCOM but only
if (and when) there is no realistic prospect of resolving the dispute without
referring it.

28.1.362AT.4

OFCOM may invite any one or more of the parties to the dispute to make a
reference under  subsection (3) .

28.1.362AT.5

OFCOM—

28.1.362AT.5.a

may impose requirements about the manner in which a reference must be made by
publishing a notice setting out those requirements,

28.1.362AT.5.b

may withdraw or modify any requirements that have been imposed by publishing a
further notice, and

28.1.362AT.5.c

in exercising their powers under  paragraph (a)  or  (b) , may make different
provision for different cases.

28.1.362AT.6

OFCOM may publish a notice under  subsection (5)  in such ways as they
consider appropriate for bringing the notice to the attention of those who, in
their opinion, are likely to be affected by it.

############ Action by OFCOM on reference of dispute

28.1.362AU

28.1.362AU.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AU.1.a

a dispute is referred to OFCOM under  section 362AT (3) , and

28.1.362AU.1.b

any requirements imposed by OFCOM under  section 362AT (5)  are met in
relation to the reference.

28.1.362AU.2

OFCOM must decide whether or not it is appropriate for them to handle the
dispute.

28.1.362AU.3

Subsection (4)  applies where—

28.1.362AU.3.a

the dispute is of the kind described in  section 362AT (1) (a)  (disputes
between the provider of a designated internet programme service and the
provider of a regulated television selection service about the arrangements
that should be made between them for the purposes of their prominence duties),
and

28.1.362AU.3.b

unless the dispute is resolved, it is highly likely that the designated
internet programme service will—

28.1.362AU.3.b.i

not be included in the regulated television selection service, or

28.1.362AU.3.b.ii

not be given the appropriate degree of prominence within it.

28.1.362AU.4

OFCOM must decide that it is appropriate for them to handle the dispute unless
they consider—

28.1.362AU.4.a

that there are alternative means available for resolving the dispute,

28.1.362AU.4.b

that a resolution by those means is likely to result in an outcome that is
consistent with the agreement objectives, and

28.1.362AU.4.c

that a prompt and satisfactory resolution of the dispute is likely if those
alternative means are used.

28.1.362AU.5

As soon as reasonably practicable after OFCOM have decided whether or not it
is appropriate for them to handle the dispute, they must inform each of the
parties to the dispute of—

28.1.362AU.5.a

their decision and the date on which it was made, and

28.1.362AU.5.b

their reasons for it.

28.1.362AU.6

Where OFCOM decide that it is not appropriate for them to handle the dispute,
the dispute may subsequently be referred back to OFCOM by one or more of the
parties if—

28.1.362AU.6.a

the parties have used alternative means for resolving the dispute but it has
not been resolved within a reasonable period of time, or

28.1.362AU.6.b

the parties have not used alternative means for resolving the dispute but
OFCOM consider that there is a satisfactory explanation for that.

############ Interim measures

28.1.362AV

28.1.362AV.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AV.1.a

OFCOM decide under  section 362AU (2)  whether or not it is appropriate for
them to handle a dispute, or

28.1.362AV.1.b

a dispute is referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) .

28.1.362AV.2

OFCOM may do one or more of the following—

28.1.362AV.2.a

make an interim declaration setting out the rights and obligations of the
parties to the dispute;

28.1.362AV.2.b

give an interim direction fixing the terms or conditions of transactions
between the parties to the dispute;

28.1.362AV.2.c

give an interim direction imposing an obligation on the parties to the
dispute, and enforceable by them, to enter into a transaction between
themselves on the terms and conditions fixed by OFCOM.

28.1.362AV.3

OFCOM must exercise their powers under  subsection (2)  in the way that seems
to them to be most appropriate in the light of the agreement objectives.

28.1.362AV.4

Before exercising their powers under  subsection (2) , OFCOM must—

28.1.362AV.4.a

give the parties to the dispute an opportunity to make representations about
the exercise of those powers, and

28.1.362AV.4.b

consider those representations.

28.1.362AV.5

In other respects, the procedure to be followed by OFCOM in connection with
the exercise of their powers under  subsection (2)  is to be the procedure
that OFCOM consider appropriate.

28.1.362AV.6

In the case of a dispute referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) ,
OFCOM may, in exercising their powers under  subsection (2) , take account of
decisions already made by others in the course of an attempt to resolve that
dispute by alternative means.

28.1.362AV.7

OFCOM must withdraw an interim declaration or an interim direction if
requested to do so by the parties to the dispute.

28.1.362AV.8

OFCOM may withdraw an interim declaration or an interim direction otherwise
than at the request of the parties to the dispute if they consider that it is
appropriate to do so in the light of the agreement objectives.

28.1.362AV.9

An interim declaration or an interim direction binds the parties to the
dispute (unless withdrawn by OFCOM or ceasing to have effect under  section
362AY (4) ).

28.1.362AV.10

In this section—

28.1.362AV.10.a

“ an interim declaration ” means a declaration that has effect until the
resolution of the dispute by OFCOM or by any alternative means (unless
withdrawn by OFCOM or ceasing to have effect under  section 362AY (4) );

28.1.362AV.10.b

“ an interim direction ” means a direction that has effect until the
resolution of the dispute by OFCOM or by any alternative means (unless
withdrawn by OFCOM or ceasing to have effect under  section 362AY (4) ).

############ Procedure for resolving disputes

28.1.362AW

28.1.362AW.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AW.1.a

OFCOM decide under  section 362AU (2)  that it is appropriate for them to
handle a dispute, or

28.1.362AW.1.b

a dispute is referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) .

28.1.362AW.2

OFCOM must—

28.1.362AW.2.a

consider the dispute, and

28.1.362AW.2.b

make a determination for resolving it.

28.1.362AW.3

The procedure for the consideration and determination of the dispute is to be
the procedure that OFCOM consider appropriate.

28.1.362AW.4

In the case of a dispute referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) ,
that procedure may involve allowing the continuation of a procedure that has
already begun for resolving the dispute by alternative means.

28.1.362AW.5

Unless there are exceptional circumstances, OFCOM must make their
determination before the end of the period of four months beginning with—

28.1.362AW.5.a

where OFCOM decide under  section 362AU (2)  that it is appropriate for them
to handle the dispute, the day on which they make that decision;

28.1.362AW.5.b

where the dispute is referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) , the day
on which it is referred back.

28.1.362AW.6

Where it is practicable for OFCOM to make their determination before the end
of the period of four months referred to in  subsection (5) , they must make
it as soon in that period as is practicable.

28.1.362AW.7

The requirements of subsections  (5)  and  (6)  are subject to  section 362AY
(4) .

28.1.362AW.8

OFCOM must—

28.1.362AW.8.a

send a copy of their determination, together with a full statement of their
reasons for it, to every party to the dispute, and

28.1.362AW.8.b

publish so much of their determination as (having regard, in particular, to
the need to preserve commercial confidentiality) they consider it appropriate
to publish.

28.1.362AW.9

OFCOM may fulfil their duty under  subsection (8) (b)  in such ways as they
consider appropriate for bringing the material that they consider it
appropriate to publish to the attention of members of the public.

############ Resolution of referred disputes

28.1.362AX

28.1.362AX.1

This section applies where OFCOM make a determination for resolving a dispute
under  section 362AW (2) .

28.1.362AX.2

OFCOM may do one or more of the following—

28.1.362AX.2.a

make a declaration setting out the rights and obligations of the parties to
the dispute;

28.1.362AX.2.b

give a direction fixing the terms or conditions of transactions between the
parties to the dispute;

28.1.362AX.2.c

give a direction imposing an obligation on the parties to the dispute, and
enforceable by them, to enter into a transaction between themselves on the
terms and conditions fixed by OFCOM;

28.1.362AX.2.d

for the purpose of giving effect to a determination by OFCOM of the proper
amount of a charge in respect of which amounts have been paid by one of the
parties to the dispute to the other, to give a direction, enforceable by the
party to whom the sums are to be paid, requiring the payment of sums by way of
adjustment of an underpayment or overpayment.

28.1.362AX.3

OFCOM must exercise their powers under  subsection (2)  in the way that they
consider to be the most appropriate for meeting the agreement objectives.

28.1.362AX.4

In the case of a dispute referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) —

28.1.362AX.4.a

OFCOM may, in making their determination, take account of decisions already
made by others in the course of an attempt to resolve that dispute by
alternative means, and

28.1.362AX.4.b

the determination made by OFCOM may include provision ratifying such
decisions.

28.1.362AX.5

Where OFCOM make a determination for resolving a dispute, they may require a
party to the dispute—

28.1.362AX.5.a

to make payments to another party to the dispute in respect of costs and
expenses incurred by that other party in consequence of the reference of the
dispute to OFCOM or in connection with it;

28.1.362AX.5.b

to make payments to OFCOM in respect of costs and expenses incurred by them in
dealing with the dispute.

28.1.362AX.6

OFCOM may determine—

28.1.362AX.6.a

the amount of any costs or expenses required to be paid under  subsection (5)
(a)  or  (b) , and

28.1.362AX.6.b

when those costs or expenses are to be paid.

28.1.362AX.7

OFCOM may not require a party to the dispute to make payments to another party
or to OFCOM under  subsection (5)  unless they have considered—

28.1.362AX.7.a

the conduct of the party before and after the reference to OFCOM (including,
in particular, whether any attempts have been made to resolve the dispute),
and

28.1.362AX.7.b

whether OFCOM have made a decision in the party’s favour in respect of the
whole or a part of the dispute.

28.1.362AX.8

A determination made by OFCOM for resolving a dispute referred to them under
section 362AT (3) , or referred back to them under  section 362AU (6) , binds
the parties to the dispute.

############ Effect of referrals on legal proceedings

28.1.362AY

28.1.362AY.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AY.1.a

a dispute is referred to OFCOM under  section 362AT (3) , or

28.1.362AY.1.b

a dispute is referred back to OFCOM under  section 362AU (6) .

28.1.362AY.2

The reference, or reference back, does not prevent the person making it, the
other party to the dispute, OFCOM or any other person from bringing, or
continuing, any legal proceedings with respect to any of the matters under
dispute.

28.1.362AY.3

The reference, or reference back, also does not prevent OFCOM from—

28.1.362AY.3.a

giving a notification in respect of something that they have reasonable
grounds for believing to be a contravention of an obligation imposed by or
under an enactment;

28.1.362AY.3.b

exercising any of their powers under any enactment in relation to a
contravention of an obligation imposed by or under an enactment;

28.1.362AY.3.c

taking any other step in preparation for, or with a view to, doing anything
mentioned in the preceding paragraphs.

28.1.362AY.4

If, in any legal proceedings with respect to a matter to which a dispute
relates, the court orders the handling of the dispute by OFCOM to be stayed or
sisted—

28.1.362AY.4.a

OFCOM are required to make a determination for resolving the dispute only if
the stay or sist is lifted or expires,

28.1.362AY.4.b

the period during which the stay or sist is in force must be disregarded in
determining the period within which OFCOM are required to make a
determination, and

28.1.362AY.4.c

any interim declaration or interim direction made or given by OFCOM under
section 362AV (2)  ceases to have effect.

28.1.362AY.5

In this section, “ legal proceedings ” means civil or criminal proceedings in
or before a court.

28.1.362AY.6

Subsection (2)  is subject to—

28.1.362AY.6.a

section 362AX (8) , and

28.1.362AY.6.b

any agreement to the contrary binding the parties in dispute.

########### Enforcement

############ Provisional notices of contravention

28.1.362AZ

28.1.362AZ.1

OFCOM may give a notice under this section (a “provisional notice of
contravention”) to a person if they consider that there are reasonable grounds
for believing that the person has failed, or is failing, to comply with—

28.1.362AZ.1.a

any duty under  section 362AD ,  362AJ  or  362AN  (duties of providers of
designated internet programme services under this Part), or

28.1.362AZ.1.b

any duty under  section 362AH ,  362AK  or  362AO  (duties of providers of
regulated television selection services under this Part).

28.1.362AZ.2

OFCOM may also give a provisional notice of contravention to a person to whom
an information notice has been given if they consider that there are
reasonable grounds for believing that the person has failed, or is failing, to
comply with the duty under  section 362AS (9) .

28.1.362AZ.3

A provisional notice of contravention must—

28.1.362AZ.3.a

specify the duty as regards which (in OFCOM’s opinion) there are reasonable
grounds for believing the person has failed, or is failing, to comply, and

28.1.362AZ.3.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for that opinion.

28.1.362AZ.4

A provisional notice of contravention may also specify steps that OFCOM
consider the person needs to take in order to—

28.1.362AZ.4.a

comply with the duty, or

28.1.362AZ.4.b

remedy the failure to comply with it.

28.1.362AZ.5

A provisional notice of contravention may also state that OFCOM propose to
impose a penalty on the person and, in such a case, the notice must—

28.1.362AZ.5.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for proposing to impose the penalty,

28.1.362AZ.5.b

indicate the amount in sterling of the penalty that is being proposed, and

28.1.362AZ.5.c

give OFCOM’s reasons for proposing a penalty of that amount, including any
aggravating or mitigating factors that OFCOM propose to take into account.

28.1.362AZ.6

A provisional notice of contravention must—

28.1.362AZ.6.a

state that the person may make representations to OFCOM (with any supporting
evidence) about the matters contained in the notice, and

28.1.362AZ.6.b

specify the period within which such representations may be made.

28.1.362AZ.7

A provisional notice of contravention may be given in respect of a failure by
the same person to comply with more than one duty and, in such a case, the
notice may include a proposal to impose a single penalty in respect of some or
all of those duties (as an alternative to separate penalties).

28.1.362AZ.8

Where a provisional notice of contravention is given in respect of a
continuing failure to comply with a duty, the notice—

28.1.362AZ.8.a

may be given in respect of any period during which the failure has continued,

28.1.362AZ.8.b

must specify that period, and

28.1.362AZ.8.c

may include a proposal to impose no more than one penalty in respect of that
period.

28.1.362AZ.9

Where a provisional notice of contravention is given to a person in respect of
a failure to comply with a duty, a further provisional notice of contravention
in respect of a failure to comply with that same duty may be given to that
person only—

28.1.362AZ.9.a

in respect of a separate instance of the failure that occurs after the first
notice is given,

28.1.362AZ.9.b

where a period is specified in the first notice in accordance with  subsection
(8) (b) , in respect of the continuation of the failure after the end of that
period, or

28.1.362AZ.9.c

if the notice is withdrawn without a confirmation decision under  section
362AZ1  having been given to the person in respect of that failure.

28.1.362AZ.10

OFCOM may give a provisional notice of contravention to—

28.1.362AZ.10.a

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a regulated television
selection service, or

28.1.362AZ.10.b

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a designated internet
programme service,

if that person was a provider of a regulated television selection service or
(as the case may be) a designated internet programme service at the time of
the failure to which the notice relates.

############ Confirmation decisions: general

28.1.362AZ1

28.1.362AZ1.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AZ1.1.a

OFCOM have given a provisional notice of contravention to a person in relation
to a failure to comply with a duty or duties, and

28.1.362AZ1.1.b

the period allowed for representations has expired.

28.1.362AZ1.2

After considering any representations that have been made (and any supporting
evidence), OFCOM must decide whether or not to give the person a further
notice under this section (a “confirmation decision”).

28.1.362AZ1.3

OFCOM may decide to give a person a confirmation decision only if they are
satisfied that the person has failed, or has been failing, to comply with the
notified duty or (as the case may be) one or more of the notified duties.

28.1.362AZ1.4

For the purposes of this section and sections  362AZ2  and  362AZ3 , a “
notified duty ” means a duty specified in the provisional notice of
contravention.

28.1.362AZ1.5

If OFCOM decide not to give a person a confirmation decision (whether because
they are not satisfied as described in  subsection (3)  or for any other
reason), they must inform the person of that fact.

28.1.362AZ1.6

A confirmation decision must—

28.1.362AZ1.6.a

state that OFCOM are satisfied that the person has failed, or has been
failing, to comply with one or more notified duties, and

28.1.362AZ1.6.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for being satisfied as described in  paragraph (a) .

28.1.362AZ1.7

A confirmation decision may require the person to take such steps as OFCOM
consider appropriate for either or both of the following purposes—

28.1.362AZ1.7.a

complying with a notified duty or duties;

28.1.362AZ1.7.b

remedying the failure to comply with that duty or those duties.

28.1.362AZ1.8

Where a provisional notice of contravention stated that OFCOM proposed to
impose a penalty in relation to a notified duty or (by virtue of  section
362AZ (7) ) in relation to notified duties, a confirmation decision may
require the person to pay a penalty, of an amount in sterling determined by
OFCOM, in relation to that duty or (as the case may be) those duties.

28.1.362AZ1.9

The amount determined by OFCOM under  subsection (8)  may be greater than the
amount indicated in the provisional notice of contravention in accordance with
section 362AZ (5) (b) .

28.1.362AZ1.10

OFCOM may give a confirmation decision to—

28.1.362AZ1.10.a

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a regulated television
selection service, or

28.1.362AZ1.10.b

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a designated internet
programme service,

if that person was a provider of a regulated television selection service or
(as the case may be) a designated internet programme service at the time of
the failure to which the notice relates.

############ Confirmation decisions: steps

28.1.362AZ2

28.1.362AZ2.1

This section applies where a confirmation decision requires the person to whom
it is given to take steps as provided for by  section 362AZ1 (7) .

28.1.362AZ2.2

The notice must—

28.1.362AZ2.2.a

specify the steps that are required and the notified duty or duties to which
each relates,

28.1.362AZ2.2.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for requiring those steps to be taken,

28.1.362AZ2.2.c

specify a reasonable period within which each of the steps specified in the
notice must be taken, and

28.1.362AZ2.2.d

contain information about the consequences of not taking the steps (including
information about further kinds of enforcement action that it would be open to
OFCOM to take).

28.1.362AZ2.3

Where a confirmation decision requires a person to take steps, the person to
whom the notice is given has a duty to take those steps.

28.1.362AZ2.4

The duty under  subsection (3)  is enforceable in civil proceedings by OFCOM—

28.1.362AZ2.4.a

for an injunction;

28.1.362AZ2.4.b

for specific performance of a statutory duty under section 45 of the Court of
Session Act 1988;

28.1.362AZ2.4.c

for any other appropriate remedy or relief.

############ Confirmation decisions: penalties

28.1.362AZ3

28.1.362AZ3.1

This section applies where a confirmation decision imposes one or more
penalties (see  section 362AZ1 (8) ).

28.1.362AZ3.2

In relation to each penalty imposed, the notice must—

28.1.362AZ3.2.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

28.1.362AZ3.2.b

specify each notified duty to which the penalty relates,

28.1.362AZ3.2.c

give OFCOM’s reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating
or mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

28.1.362AZ3.2.d

specify a reasonable period within which the penalty must be paid, and

28.1.362AZ3.2.e

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the kinds of enforcement action that it would be
open to OFCOM to take).

28.1.362AZ3.3

The period specified under  subsection (2) (d)  for the payment of a penalty
must be at least 28 days beginning with the day on which the confirmation
decision is given.

28.1.362AZ3.4

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a confirmation decision.

############ Penalty for failure to comply with confirmation decisions

28.1.362AZ4

28.1.362AZ4.1

This section applies where—

28.1.362AZ4.1.a

OFCOM have given a confirmation decision to a person,

28.1.362AZ4.1.b

the notice includes requirements to take steps (as provided for by  section
362AZ1 (7) ), and

28.1.362AZ4.1.c

OFCOM are satisfied that the person has failed to comply with one or more of
those requirements.

28.1.362AZ4.2

OFCOM may give the person a penalty notice.

28.1.362AZ4.3

A “penalty notice” is a notice requiring a person to pay to OFCOM a penalty of
an amount in sterling determined by OFCOM.

28.1.362AZ4.4

Before giving the person a penalty notice, OFCOM must—

28.1.362AZ4.4.a

notify the person that they propose to give a penalty notice in respect of the
failure to comply with the confirmation decision, specifying the reasons for
their proposal and indicating the amount of the proposed penalty, and

28.1.362AZ4.4.b

give the person an opportunity to make representations to OFCOM (with any
supporting evidence) about their proposal.

28.1.362AZ4.5

A penalty notice must—

28.1.362AZ4.5.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

28.1.362AZ4.5.b

state the amount of the penalty,

28.1.362AZ4.5.c

state the reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating or
mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

28.1.362AZ4.5.d

specify the period within which the penalty must be paid, and

28.1.362AZ4.5.e

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the further kinds of enforcement action that it
would be open to OFCOM to take).

28.1.362AZ4.6

The period specified under  subsection (5) (d)  must be at least 28 days
beginning with the day on which the penalty notice is given.

28.1.362AZ4.7

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a penalty notice.

############ Enforcement: guidance

28.1.362AZ5

28.1.362AZ5.1

OFCOM must prepare and publish guidance about the exercise of their powers
under sections  362AZ  to  362AZ4  and  Schedule 16B  (so far as relating to
this Part).

28.1.362AZ5.2

The guidance must include the factors that OFCOM will take into account in
deciding whether to exercise any of those powers.

28.1.362AZ5.3

OFCOM may revise or replace any guidance published under this section and,
where they do so, must publish the revised or replacement guidance.

28.1.362AZ5.4

Before preparing guidance under this section (or revising or replacing it),
OFCOM must consult—

28.1.362AZ5.4.a

the Secretary of State, and

28.1.362AZ5.4.b

such other persons as they consider appropriate.

28.1.362AZ5.5

Guidelines prepared by OFCOM under section 392 (amount of penalties) may, so
far as relating to penalties imposed by a confirmation decision under  section
362AZ1  or a penalty notice under section  362AZ4 , be included in the same
document as guidance under this section.

28.1.362AZ5.6

In exercising or deciding whether to exercise any of their powers under
sections  362AZ  to  362AZ4  and  Schedule 16B  (so far as relating to this
Part), OFCOM must have regard to any guidance for the time being published
under this section.

########### Supplemental provisions of Part 3A

############ Fees

28.1.362AZ6

28.1.362AZ6.1

OFCOM may require a person other than the BBC or S4C who is—

28.1.362AZ6.1.a

a provider of a designated internet programme service, or

28.1.362AZ6.1.b

a provider of a regulated television selection service,

to pay to OFCOM a fee of an amount determined by OFCOM.

28.1.362AZ6.2

The amount of a fee required under  subsection (1)  must be determined by
OFCOM in accordance with a statement of principles prepared and published by
them for the purpose of this section.

28.1.362AZ6.3

Those principles must be such as appear to OFCOM to be likely to secure the
following objectives—

28.1.362AZ6.3.a

that, on a year by year basis, the aggregate amount of the fees payable to
OFCOM under  subsection (1)  is sufficient to meet, but does not exceed, the
annual cost to OFCOM of carrying out their functions under this Part less an
appropriate amount to take into account costs that will be met by fees
payable—

28.1.362AZ6.3.a.i

by the BBC under section 198(4), or

28.1.362AZ6.3.a.ii

by S4C under section 207(6);

28.1.362AZ6.3.b

that the relationship between the aggregate amount of the fees and the cost to
OFCOM of carrying out the functions is transparent;

28.1.362AZ6.3.c

that any fee required is justifiable and proportionate having regard to the
circumstances of the person required to pay it.

28.1.362AZ6.4

As soon as reasonably practicable after the end of each financial year, OFCOM
must publish a statement of accounts setting out in respect of that year—

28.1.362AZ6.4.a

the aggregate amount of the fees payable under  subsection (1)  for that year
that have been received by OFCOM,

28.1.362AZ6.4.b

the aggregate amount of the fees payable under  subsection (1)  for that year
that remain outstanding and are likely to be paid or recovered, and

28.1.362AZ6.4.c

the costs to them of carrying out their functions under this Part less an
appropriate amount to take into account costs that have been or are to be met
by fees payable—

28.1.362AZ6.4.c.i

by the BBC under section 198(4), or

28.1.362AZ6.4.c.ii

by S4C under section 207(6).

28.1.362AZ6.5

Any deficit or surplus shown (after applying this subsection for all previous
years) by the statement of accounts is to be—

28.1.362AZ6.5.a

carried forward, and

28.1.362AZ6.5.b

taken into account in determining what is required to meet the objective
described in  subsection (3) (a)  in relation to the following year.

28.1.362AZ6.6

OFCOM may repay a person some or all of a fee paid under  subsection (1)  if—

28.1.362AZ6.6.a

in the case of a fee paid by the provider of a designated internet programme
service, OFCOM revoke the designation of an internet programme service
provided by that person under  section 362AB  at some time during the period
to which the fee relates;

28.1.362AZ6.6.b

in the case of a fee paid by the provider of a regulated television selection
service—

28.1.362AZ6.6.b.i

the Secretary of State has revoked the designation of a regulated television
selection service provided by that person at some time during the period to
which the fee relates, or

28.1.362AZ6.6.b.ii

the person gives OFCOM a notice under  section 362AH (2)  or  (3)  in
accordance with  section 362AH (4)  at some time during the period to which
the fee relates.

28.1.362AZ6.7

For the purposes of this section, OFCOM’s costs of carrying out their
functions under this Part during a financial year include their costs of
preparing to carry out those functions during that year.

28.1.362AZ6.8

OFCOM—

28.1.362AZ6.8.a

may revise a statement of principles published by them, and

28.1.362AZ6.8.b

where they do so, must publish the statement as revised.

28.1.362AZ6.9

Before publishing a statement of principles or a revision of it, OFCOM must
consult such persons as they consider appropriate.

28.1.362AZ6.10

In this section, a reference to the functions of OFCOM under this Part
includes a reference to their functions under  Schedules 16A  and  16B , so
far as relating to this Part.

28.1.362AZ6.11

In this section, “ financial year ” means a period of 12 months ending on 31
March.

############ Non-payment of fee

28.1.362AZ7

28.1.362AZ7.1

This section applies if—

28.1.362AZ7.1.a

the provider of a designated internet programme service or regulated
television selection service is liable to pay a fee to OFCOM under  section
362AZ6 , and

28.1.362AZ7.1.b

in OFCOM’s opinion, the provider has not paid the full amount of the fee that
the provider is liable to pay.

28.1.362AZ7.2

OFCOM may give the provider a notice under this subsection specifying—

28.1.362AZ7.2.a

the outstanding amount of the fee that OFCOM consider the provider is due to
pay to them under  section 362AZ6 , and

28.1.362AZ7.2.b

the period within which the provider must pay it.

28.1.362AZ7.3

A notice under  subsection (2) —

28.1.362AZ7.3.a

may relate to fees required on different occasions;

28.1.362AZ7.3.b

may also state that OFCOM propose to impose a penalty on the provider.

28.1.362AZ7.4

The provider may make representations to OFCOM (with any supporting evidence)
about the matters contained in the notice.

28.1.362AZ7.5

Subsection (6)  applies if—

28.1.362AZ7.5.a

the notice under  subsection (2)  stated that OFCOM propose to impose a
penalty,

28.1.362AZ7.5.b

the period allowed for representations has expired, and

28.1.362AZ7.5.c

OFCOM are satisfied that an amount of the fee or fees is still due to them.

28.1.362AZ7.6

OFCOM may give the provider a penalty notice under this subsection requiring
the provider to pay to OFCOM a penalty of an amount in sterling determined by
OFCOM.

28.1.362AZ7.7

The penalty may consist of any of the following—

28.1.362AZ7.7.a

a single amount;

28.1.362AZ7.7.b

an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate;

28.1.362AZ7.7.c

a combination of a single amount and an amount calculated by reference to a
daily rate.

28.1.362AZ7.8

The penalty notice may impose a penalty of a different kind, of a greater
amount or (in the case of a penalty calculated by reference to a daily rate)
payable over a longer period than that proposed in the notice about the
proposed penalty.

28.1.362AZ7.9

See  section 362AZ8  for information which must be included in notices under
this section.

28.1.362AZ7.10

Nothing in this section affects OFCOM’s power to bring proceedings (whether
before or after the imposition of a penalty by a notice under  subsection (6)
) for the recovery of the whole or part of an amount due to OFCOM under
section 362AZ6 .

28.1.362AZ7.11

But OFCOM may not bring such proceedings unless a provider has first been
given a notice under  subsection (2)  specifying the amount due to OFCOM.

############ Information to be included in a notice under 

28.1.362AZ8

28.1.362AZ8.1

A notice under  section 362AZ7 (2)  stating that OFCOM propose to impose a
penalty must—

28.1.362AZ8.1.a

state the reasons why OFCOM propose to impose the penalty,

28.1.362AZ8.1.b

state whether OFCOM propose that the penalty should consist of a single
amount, an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, or a combination of
the two,

28.1.362AZ8.1.c

indicate the amount of the proposed penalty, including (in relation to an
amount calculated by reference to a daily rate) the daily rate and how the
penalty would be calculated,

28.1.362AZ8.1.d

in relation to an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, specify or
describe the period for which OFCOM propose that the amount should be payable,

28.1.362AZ8.1.e

state the reasons for proposing a penalty of that amount, including any
aggravating or mitigating factors that OFCOM propose to take into account, and

28.1.362AZ8.1.f

specify the period within which representations in relation to the proposed
penalty may be made.

28.1.362AZ8.2

A penalty notice under  section 362AZ7 (6)  must—

28.1.362AZ8.2.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

28.1.362AZ8.2.b

state whether the penalty consists of a single amount, an amount calculated by
reference to a daily rate, or a combination of the two, and how it is
calculated,

28.1.362AZ8.2.c

in relation to a single amount, state that amount,

28.1.362AZ8.2.d

in relation to an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, state the
daily rate,

28.1.362AZ8.2.e

state the reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating or
mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

28.1.362AZ8.2.f

specify a reasonable period within which the penalty must be paid, and

28.1.362AZ8.2.g

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the further kinds of enforcement action that it
would be open to OFCOM to take).

28.1.362AZ8.3

A penalty notice under  section 362AZ7 (6)  must also specify the amount of
the fee that is (in OFCOM’s opinion) due to be paid to OFCOM.

28.1.362AZ8.4

The period specified under  subsection (2) (f)  for the payment of a single
amount must be at least 28 days beginning with the day on which the penalty
notice is given.

28.1.362AZ8.5

Subsection (6)  applies in relation to a penalty notice under  section 362AZ7
(6)  that includes a requirement to pay an amount calculated by reference to a
daily rate.

28.1.362AZ8.6

Such a notice must—

28.1.362AZ8.6.a

state the date from which the amount begins to be payable, which must not be
earlier than the day after the day on which the notice is given;

28.1.362AZ8.6.b

provide for the amount to continue to be payable at the daily rate until—

28.1.362AZ8.6.b.i

the date on which the full amount of the fee (as specified in the penalty
notice) has been paid to OFCOM, or

28.1.362AZ8.6.b.ii

an earlier date specified in the penalty notice.

28.1.362AZ8.7

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a penalty notice under  section 362AZ7 (6) .

############ Monitoring role for OFCOM

28.1.362AZ9

OFCOM have the function of obtaining, compiling and keeping under review
information about matters which may be relevant to—

28.1.362AZ9.a

designating or revoking the designation of an internet programme service under
section 362AA  or  362AB ;

28.1.362AZ9.b

designating or revoking the designation of a television selection service or
specifying or ceasing to specify a description of television selection
services under  section 362AF ;

28.1.362AZ9.c

deciding whether to take enforcement action under this Part and Schedule 16B
(so far as relating to this Part).

############ Notices

28.1.362AZ10

28.1.362AZ10.1

This section applies in relation to a notice that may or must be given by
OFCOM to a person under any provision of this Part or Schedule 16B (so far as
relating to this Part).

28.1.362AZ10.2

OFCOM may give a notice to a person by—

28.1.362AZ10.2.a

delivering it by hand to the person,

28.1.362AZ10.2.b

leaving it at the person’s proper address,

28.1.362AZ10.2.c

sending it by post to the person at that address, or

28.1.362AZ10.2.d

sending it by email to that person’s email address.

28.1.362AZ10.3

A notice to a body corporate may be given to any officer of that body.

28.1.362AZ10.4

A notice to a partnership may be given to any partner or to a person who has
the control or management of the partnership business.

28.1.362AZ10.5

A notice to an entity that is not a legal person under the law under which it
is formed (other than a partnership) may be given to any member of the
governing body of the entity.

28.1.362AZ10.6

In the case of a notice given to a person who is a provider of a regulated
television selection service, the person’s proper address for the purposes of
paragraphs (b) and (c) of subsection (2), and section 7 of the Interpretation
Act 1978 in its application to those paragraphs, is any address (within or
outside the United Kingdom) at which OFCOM believe, on reasonable grounds,
that the notice will come to the attention of the person or (where that person
is an entity) any director or other officer of that entity.

28.1.362AZ10.7

In the case of a notice given to a person other than a provider of a regulated
television selection service, a person’s proper address for the purposes of
paragraphs (b) and (c) of subsection (2), and section 7 of the Interpretation
Act 1978 in its application to those paragraphs, is—

28.1.362AZ10.7.a

in the case of an entity, the address of the entity’s registered or principal
office;

28.1.362AZ10.7.b

in any other case, the person’s last known address.

28.1.362AZ10.8

In the case of an entity registered or carrying on business outside the United
Kingdom, or with offices outside the United Kingdom, the reference in
subsection (7)  to its principal office includes—

28.1.362AZ10.8.a

its principal office in the United Kingdom, or

28.1.362AZ10.8.b

if the entity has no office in the United Kingdom, any place in the United
Kingdom at which OFCOM believe, on reasonable grounds, that the notice will
come to the attention of any director or other officer of that entity.

28.1.362AZ10.9

For the purposes of  subsection (2) (d) , a person’s email address is—

28.1.362AZ10.9.a

any email address published for the time being by that person as an address
for contacting that person, or

28.1.362AZ10.9.b

if there is no such published address, any email address by means of which
OFCOM believe, on reasonable grounds, that the notice will come to the
attention of that person or (where that person is an entity) any director or
other officer of that entity.

28.1.362AZ10.10

A notice sent by email is treated as given 48 hours after it was sent, unless
the contrary is proved.

28.1.362AZ10.11

In this section—

      “ director ” includes any person occupying the position of a director,
by whatever name called;           “ officer ”, in relation to an entity,
includes a director, a manager, a partner, an associate, a secretary or, where
the affairs of the entity are managed by its members, a member.

############ Application of Part 3A

28.1.362AZ11

28.1.362AZ11.1

A duty imposed on a provider of a television selection service by or under
this Part applies in relation to that service only so far as it is made
available for use by members of the public in the United Kingdom.

28.1.362AZ11.2

References in this Part to a television selection service include such a
service provided from outside the United Kingdom (as well as such a service
provided from within the United Kingdom).

28.1.362AZ11.3

References in this Part to an internet programme service include such a
service provided from outside the United Kingdom (as well as such a service
provided from within the United Kingdom).

28.1.362AZ11.4

The power to require the provision of information by an information notice
includes power to require the provision of information held outside the United
Kingdom.

28.1.362AZ11.5

Section  362AZ2 (4)  (requirements enforceable in civil proceedings against a
person) applies whether or not the person is in the United Kingdom.

############ Interpretation of Part 3A

28.1.362AZ12

28.1.362AZ12.1

In this Part—

      “ the agreement objectives ” has the meaning given by  section 362AM ;
“ BBC company ”, “ C4 company ” and “ S4C company ” have the same meaning as
in Part 3 (see section 362);           “ designated internet programme service
” has the meaning given by  section 362AA ;           “ entity ” means a body
or association of persons or an organisation, regardless of whether the body,
association or organisation is—         formed under the law of any part of
the United Kingdom or of a country or territory outside the United Kingdom, or
a legal person under the law under which it is formed;                 “
information notice ” has the meaning given by  section 362AS ;           “
internet programme service ” has the meaning given by  section 362AA ;
“ licensed public service channel ” has the same meaning as in Part 3 (see
section 362);           “ listed channel ” has the meaning given by  section
362AM ;           “ programme ” means such programme as is described in
section 368ZA;           “ provision ”—         in relation to an internet
programme service, is to be construed in accordance with  subsection (2) ;
in relation to a television selection service, is to be construed in
accordance with  section 362AE (5) ;                 “ public service
broadcaster ” has the meaning given by section 264;           “ public service
remit ” has the meaning given by  section 362AA ;           “ public service
remit content ” has the meaning given by  section 362AA ;           “
regulated television selection service ” has the meaning given by  section
362AF ;           “ television selection service ” has the meaning given by
section 362AE .

28.1.362AZ12.2

The person, and the only person, who is to be treated for the purposes of this
Part as providing an internet programme service is the person who has general
control of the service.

28.1.362AZ12.3

In the case of an internet programme service where the programmes provided to
a user of the service are contained in a single on-demand programme service,
the person with general control of the service is the person who has editorial
responsibility for the on-demand programme service (see section 368A(4)).

28.1.362AZ12.4

In the case of any other internet programme service, the person with general
control of the service is the person who has general control over which—

28.1.362AZ12.4.a

on-demand programme services,

28.1.362AZ12.4.b

non-UK on-demand programme services, and

28.1.362AZ12.4.c

services that fall within  section 362AA (10) (c) ,

are included in the service.

28.1.362AZ12.5

For the purposes of this Part—

28.1.362AZ12.5.a

the provision of an internet programme service by the BBC does not include its
provision by a BBC company;

28.1.362AZ12.5.b

the provision of an internet programme service by C4C does not include its
provision by a C4 company;

28.1.362AZ12.5.c

the provision of an internet programme service by S4C does not include its
provision by an S4C company;

and, accordingly, control that is or is capable of being exercised by the BBC,
C4C or S4C over decisions by a BBC company, C4 company or S4C company about
what is to be comprised in a service is to be disregarded for the purposes of
determining who has general control of the service.

28.1.362AZ12.6

For the purposes of this Part, a person (“ P ”) is associated with a public
service broadcaster if, and only if—

28.1.362AZ12.6.a

P is a body corporate which is controlled by the public service broadcaster;
or

28.1.362AZ12.6.b

where the public service broadcaster is the provider of a Channel 3 service or
Channel 5, P and the public service broadcaster are bodies corporate which are
both controlled by the same person.

28.1.362AZ12.7

In  subsection (6)  “ controlled ” has the same meaning as in Part 1 of
Schedule 2 to the 1990 Act.

28.1.362AZ12.8

A reference in this Part to access, in relation to a programme provided by an
internet programme service, is a reference to the opportunity of viewing in an
intelligible form a programme so provided.

28.1.362AZ12.9

For the purposes of this Part, a reference to an internet programme service
being included in a television selection service is a reference to being one
of the internet programme services that are, or whose programmes are,
available for selection and access by means of the television selection
service.

28.1.362AZ12.10

The services that are to be taken for the purposes of this Part to be
available for use by members of the public include any service which—

28.1.362AZ12.10.a

is made available for use only by persons who subscribe to the service
(whether for a period or in relation to a particular occasion) or who
otherwise request its provision, but

28.1.362AZ12.10.b

is a service the facility of subscribing to which, or of otherwise requesting
its provision, is offered or made available to members of the public.

28.2

Schedule 3  contains further amendments relating to prominence on television
selection services.

### Public service broadcasters

#### C4C

##### Sustainability duty of C4C

29

29.1

The Broadcasting Act 1990 is amended as follows.

29.2

After section 23 insert—

########### Sustainability duty of Corporation

29.2.23A

29.2.23A.1

The Corporation must carry on their activities in the way that they have
reasonable grounds to consider would be most likely to enable the Corporation,
over the long term—

29.2.23A.1.a

to maintain or increase the amount of activity that is done in pursuance of
their primary functions, and

29.2.23A.1.b

to be securely in a position to meet costs incurred in the carrying out of
their primary functions.

29.2.23A.2

In this section, “ primary functions ” has the same meaning as in section
199(1) of the Communications Act 2003.

29.3

In Schedule 3 (the Channel Four Television Corporation: supplementary
provisions), in paragraph 13 (annual reports), after sub-paragraph (1) insert—

29.3.1A

The report must include a report on the discharge by the Corporation of their
duty under  section 23A  (sustainability duty of Corporation).

##### C4C’s duties in relation to commissioning programmes

30

30.1

The Communications Act 2003 is amended as follows.

30.2

After section 198A insert—

########### C4C’s duties in relation to commissioning programmes

30.2.198AA

30.2.198AA.1

C4C must take steps to enable competition for commissions from C4C to make
programmes, other than advertisements, for inclusion in services provided by
C4C that fall within  subsection (2) .

30.2.198AA.2

A service falls within this subsection if it is—

30.2.198AA.2.a

a television broadcasting service,

30.2.198AA.2.b

a television licensable content service,

30.2.198AA.2.c

a digital television programme service,

30.2.198AA.2.d

an on-demand programme service that is or forms part of a designated internet
programme service, or

30.2.198AA.2.e

a non-UK on-demand programme service that is or forms part of a designated
internet programme service.

30.2.198AA.3

C4C must put in place and adhere to procedures that facilitate fair
competition for such commissions, including procedures for referring disputes
with C4C to mediation.

30.2.198AA.4

In this section, “ designated internet programme service ” has the same
meaning as in Part 3A (see  section 362AZ12 ).

30.3

In section 198B (statement of media content policy)—

30.3.a

in the heading—

30.3.a.i

for “Statement” substitute  “Statements” ;

30.3.a.ii

at the end insert  “and commissioning policy” ;

30.3.b

after subsection (1) insert—

30.3.b.1A

C4C must prepare a statement of commissioning policy at the same time as they
prepare a statement of media content policy.

;

30.3.c

in subsection (2), after “policy” insert  “or commissioning policy” ;

30.3.d

after subsection (3) insert—

30.3.d.3A

A statement of commissioning policy must—

30.3.d.3A.a

set out C4C’s proposals for securing that, during the following year, they
will discharge their duties under section  198AA , and

30.3.d.3A.b

include a report on their performance in carrying out the proposals contained
in the previous statement.

;

30.3.e

in subsection (4), for “the statement” substitute  “a statement of media
content policy or commissioning policy” ;

30.3.f

in subsection (5), after “policy” insert  “or commissioning policy” .

30.4

In section 198C (OFCOM reports on C4C’s media content duties)—

30.4.a

in the heading, at the end insert  “and commissioning duties” ;

30.4.b

in subsection (1), in paragraph (a), for “section 198A” substitute  “sections
198A and  198AA ” .

30.5

In section 198D (directions in relation to C4C’s media content duties)—

30.5.a

in the heading, at the end insert  “and commissioning duties” ;

30.5.b

in subsection (1), in paragraph (a)—

30.5.b.i

after “198A” insert  “,  198AA ” ;

30.5.b.ii

for “198B(1), (3)” substitute  “198B(1), (1A), (3), (3A)” ;

30.5.c

in subsection (2)(a), after “policy” insert  “or (as the case may be)
commissioning policy” ;

30.5.d

in subsection (3)(a), after “policy” insert  “or (as the case may be)
commissioning policy” .

30.6

In section 271A (remedying failure by C4C to perform media content duties)—

30.6.a

in subsection (1)(a), after “198A” insert  “or  198AA ” ;

30.6.b

in subsection (2), after “198A” insert  “or  198AA ” .

##### Involvement of C4C in programme-making

31

31.1

In the Communications Act 2003, omit section 295 (which restricts C4C’s
involvement in programme-making).

31.2

Subsections  (3)  and  (4)  apply if, after the coming into force of
subsection (1) , C4C or a body corporate controlled by C4C engage in the
making of one or more programmes with a view to their being broadcast on
Channel 4.

31.3

In carrying out a review under section 264 of the Communications Act 2003 in
relation to the relevant report period, OFCOM must consider whether and to
what extent the making of programmes by C4C or a body corporate controlled by
C4C with a view to their being broadcast on Channel 4 has affected the
fulfilment of the public service remit for television in the United Kingdom.

31.4

The report on that review must set out the findings of OFCOM on their
consideration of the matter mentioned in  subsection (3)  and any conclusions
that they have arrived at in relation to those findings.

31.5

For the purposes of this section—

31.5.a

the relevant report period is the first report period to end on or after the
relevant day, and

31.5.b

the relevant day is the third anniversary of the first day on which, following
the coming into force of  subsection (1) , C4C or a body corporate controlled
by C4C engages in the making of a programme with a view to its being broadcast
on Channel 4.

31.6

In this section—

      “ broadcast ” has the same meaning as in the Communications Act 2003;
“ C4C ” means the Channel Four Television Corporation;           “ Channel 4 ”
has the same meaning as in Part 1 of the Broadcasting Act 1990;           “
controlled ” has the same meaning as in Part 1 of the Broadcasting Act 1990;
“ OFCOM ” means the Office of Communications;           “ programme ” means a
television programme (within the meaning of the Communications Act 2003) other
than an advertisement;           “ the public service remit for television in
the United Kingdom ” has the meaning given by section 264 of the
Communications Act 2003;           “ report period ” means a period selected
by OFCOM for the purposes of section 264(1)(b) of the Communications Act 2003.

#### S4C

##### S4C’s powers and public service remit

32

32.1

The Communications Act 2003 is amended in accordance with  subsections (2)
and  (3) .

32.2

For sections 204 to 206 (S4C’s functions and main powers), substitute—

########### S4C’s principal powers and public service remit

32.2.204A

32.2.204A.1

S4C may make available any audiovisual content.

32.2.204A.2

S4C’s public service remit is to make available a broad range of high quality
and diverse audiovisual content—

32.2.204A.2.a

a substantial proportion of which is in Welsh,

32.2.204A.2.b

which is all capable of being taken into account for the purpose of
determining the extent to which the public service remit for television in the
United Kingdom is fulfilled (see section 264(7) to (8C)), and

32.2.204A.2.c

which, considered as a whole, constitutes an adequate contribution to the
fulfilment of that remit.

32.2.204A.3

S4C must exercise the power in subsection  (1)  to fulfil its public service
remit.

32.2.204A.4

S4C may do anything it considers appropriate in association with anything it
does in exercise of the power in subsection  (1) .

32.2.204A.5

In this section “ audiovisual content ” has the same meaning as in section
264.

32.2.204A.6

Subsection  (13)  of section 264 (interpretation of “made available”) applies
for the purposes of this section as it applies for the purposes of that
section.

########### Restrictions on S4C’s powers

32.2.204B

32.2.204B.1

S4C must obtain the Secretary of State’s approval in writing before (whether
under section  204A  or otherwise)—

32.2.204B.1.a

providing any television programme services;

32.2.204B.1.b

doing anything for a charge or with a view to making a profit.

32.2.204B.2

S4C must ensure that an S4C company obtains the Secretary of State’s approval
in writing before the company does anything for a charge or with a view to
making a profit.

32.2.204B.3

An approval under this section may be—

32.2.204B.3.a

a general approval in relation to a description of activities, or

32.2.204B.3.b

a specific approval in relation to particular activities.

32.2.204B.4

For the purposes of this section, the carrying on of the following activities
is treated as approved by the Secretary of State (so far as approval under
this section would otherwise be required)—

32.2.204B.4.a

the provision of S4C Digital,

32.2.204B.4.b

each activity whose carrying on is approved under section 205 or 206 of this
Act (S4C’s other activities) immediately before this section comes into force,
and

32.2.204B.4.c

each activity which is being carried on by S4C or an S4C company immediately
before this section comes into force.

32.2.204B.5

S4C may not provide a service that would fall to be regulated under section
245 (independent radio services) if provided by an S4C company.

########### Publication of approvals under section 204B

32.2.204C

32.2.204C.1

The Secretary of State must publish any approval under section  204B , subject
to  subsection (2) .

32.2.204C.2

The Secretary of State must exclude from publication any matters which appear
to the Secretary of State to be matters whose publication would or might
seriously and prejudicially affect the interests of any person.

32.2.204C.3

This section does not apply in relation to activities treated under  section
204B (4)  as approved under that section.

32.3

In section 207 (S4C: charging and borrowing etc), omit subsections (1) and
(2).

32.4

In Schedule 6 to the Broadcasting Act 1990 (S4C: supplementary provisions), in
paragraph 1, for sub-paragraph (3) substitute—

32.4.3

In carrying out its functions S4C may carry on activities in any way whatever,
including—

32.4.3.a

through or with other persons;

32.4.3.b

anywhere in the United Kingdom or elsewhere;

32.4.3.c

with a view to making a profit;

32.4.3.d

for a charge.

##### The S4C Board

33

33.1

The Broadcasting Act 1990 is amended in accordance with subsections  (2)  to
(4) .
