33.2

In section 56 (Welsh Authority to continue in existence as S4C), for
subsection (2) substitute—

33.2.2

The members of the S4C Board (see  section 56A  and  Schedule 6A ) are to be
the members of S4C, but membership of S4C does not enable any person to act
otherwise than through the S4C Board.

33.3

After section 56 insert—

########### The S4C Board

33.3.56A

33.3.56A.1

A Board of S4C is established.

33.3.56A.2

That Board—

33.3.56A.2.a

is to be known as the S4C Board or (in Welsh) Bwrdd S4C, and

33.3.56A.2.b

is to be constituted in accordance with this Act.

33.3.56A.3

Except where otherwise provided by or under any enactment, the duties and
powers of S4C are to be discharged and exercised by the S4C Board on behalf of
S4C.

33.3.56A.4

Schedule 6A  makes further provision about the S4C Board.

33.4

After Schedule 6 insert—

  The S4C Board

Section 56A

############# Membership

33.4.1

33.4.1.1

The S4C Board is to consist of—

33.4.1.1.a

non-executive members, and

33.4.1.1.b

executive members.

33.4.1.2

The non-executive members are to be—

33.4.1.2.a

a chair, and

33.4.1.2.b

at least five, and not more than eight, other non-executive members.

33.4.1.3

It is for the Secretary of State—

33.4.1.3.a

to decide, in accordance with  sub-paragraph (2) (b) , the number of other
non-executive members;

33.4.1.3.b

to appoint the non-executive members.

33.4.1.4

The executive members are to be—

33.4.1.4.a

the employee of S4C holding the position of, or acting as, Chief Executive of
S4C, and

33.4.1.4.b

at least one and not more than two other employees of S4C.

33.4.1.5

It is for the non-executive members, in accordance with  sub-paragraph (4) (b)
—

33.4.1.5.a

to decide the number of other executive members;

33.4.1.5.b

to appoint the other executive members.

33.4.1.6

A person making an appointment under this paragraph must do so with a view to
ensuring that, collectively, the members of the S4C Board have the range of
skills and experience needed for the effective running of S4C.

33.4.2

33.4.2.1

The members of the S4C Board must not at any time include a person who is a
member or an employee of the BBC.

33.4.2.2

The members of the S4C Board must not at any time include a person who is a
member or an employee of OFCOM.

33.4.2.3

The Secretary of State must—

33.4.2.3.a

before appointing a person to be a non-executive member of the S4C Board, be
satisfied that the person will not have any financial or other interest likely
to affect prejudicially the discharge of that person’s duties as a member of
the S4C Board, and

33.4.2.3.b

from time to time consider, in respect of each non-executive member of the S4C
Board, whether that member has any such interest.

############# Tenure of office

33.4.3

33.4.3.1

A member of the S4C Board holds and vacates office in accordance with the
terms of the member’s appointment, subject to the provisions of this Schedule.

33.4.3.2

A non-executive member must be appointed for a fixed term of not more than
five years.

33.4.3.3

A person who has held office as a non-executive member for two consecutive
terms may not be re-appointed as a non-executive member until the end of the
five years beginning with the end of the second of those terms.

33.4.3.4

A non-executive member ceases to be a member of the S4C Board if the member—

33.4.3.4.a

becomes an employee of S4C, or

33.4.3.4.b

resigns from office by giving written notice to the Secretary of State.

33.4.3.5

An executive member under  paragraph 1 (4) (a)  ceases to be a member of the
S4C Board on ceasing to be the Chief Executive of S4C.

33.4.3.6

Any other executive member ceases to be a member of the S4C Board if the
member—

33.4.3.6.a

ceases to be an employee of S4C, or

33.4.3.6.b

resigns from office by giving written notice to S4C.

############# Remuneration and pensions of members

33.4.4

33.4.4.1

S4C may pay to each non-executive member of the S4C Board such remuneration
and allowances as the Secretary of State may determine.

33.4.4.2

S4C may pay or make provision for paying to or in respect of any non-executive
member of the S4C Board such sums by way of pensions, allowances or gratuities
as the Secretary of State may determine.

33.4.4.3

S4C may pay compensation, of such amount as the Secretary of State may
determine, to a person where—

33.4.4.3.a

the person ceases to be a non-executive member of the S4C Board otherwise than
on the expiry of the person’s term of office, and

33.4.4.3.b

it appears to the Secretary of State that there are special circumstances
which make it right for the person to receive compensation.

############# Proceedings

33.4.5

33.4.5.1

The S4C Board may regulate its own procedure (including quorum), subject to
the provisions of paragraphs  6  and  7 .

33.4.5.2

The S4C Board may make arrangements providing for the discharge of any of the
S4C Board’s functions by—

33.4.5.2.a

a committee, or

33.4.5.2.b

one or more persons each of whom is either a member of the S4C Board or an
employee of S4C.

33.4.6

In managing the affairs of S4C the S4C Board must have regard to such
generally accepted principles of good corporate governance as it is reasonable
to regard as applicable to S4C.

33.4.7

33.4.7.1

A member of the S4C Board who has an interest, whether directly or indirectly,
in any matter that is brought up for consideration at a meeting of the S4C
Board must disclose the nature of that interest to the meeting.

33.4.7.2

Where a disclosure is made under  sub-paragraph (1) —

33.4.7.2.a

the disclosure must be recorded in the minutes of the meeting, and

33.4.7.2.b

subject to  sub-paragraph (3) , the member must not take part in any
deliberation or decision of the S4C Board, or any of its committees, with
respect to that matter.

33.4.7.3

Sub-paragraph  (2) (b)  does not apply in relation to a meeting of the S4C
Board at which all the other members present resolve that the member’s
interest is to be disregarded for the purposes of that provision.

33.4.7.4

For the purposes of  sub-paragraph (1) —

33.4.7.4.a

a general notification given at a meeting of the S4C Board that the member is
to be regarded as interested in any matter involving a specified organisation
is to be regarded as a sufficient disclosure of the member’s interest in
relation to any such matter, and

33.4.7.4.b

a member may make a disclosure under that sub-paragraph without attending a
meeting of the S4C Board if the member takes reasonable steps to secure that
the disclosure is made by a notice which is taken into consideration and read
at a meeting.

33.4.7.5

References in this paragraph to a meeting of the S4C Board include references
to a meeting of any of its committees.

33.4.8

The validity of any proceedings of S4C or the S4C Board is not affected by—

33.4.8.a

any vacancy among the members of the S4C Board,

33.4.8.b

any defect in the appointment of a member of the S4C Board, or

33.4.8.c

a failure to comply with the requirements of  paragraph 7 .

33.5

Any person who is the chair, or one of the other members, of S4C immediately
before this section comes into force—

33.5.a

becomes the chair, or one of the other non-executive members, of the S4C Board
on the coming into force of this section, and

33.5.b

holds that office—

33.5.b.i

for the remainder of the term of the person’s appointment as chair or other
member of S4C (subject to  paragraph 3 (4)  of  Schedule 6A  to the
Broadcasting Act 1990, as inserted by  subsection (4)  of this section), and

33.5.b.ii

on and subject to the terms of that appointment.

##### Accounts and audit

34

34.1

Schedule 6 to the Broadcasting Act 1990 (S4C: supplementary provisions) is
amended as follows.

34.2

For paragraph 12(2) and (3) (audit of S4C’s accounts by appointed auditor)
substitute—

34.2.2A

S4C must send a copy of its statement of accounts to the Comptroller and
Auditor General as soon as possible after the end of the financial year to
which the statement relates.

34.2.2B

The Comptroller and Auditor General must—

34.2.2B.a

examine, certify and report on each statement of accounts of S4C, and

34.2.2B.b

send a copy of the report and certified statement of accounts to the Secretary
of State.

34.2.2C

The Secretary of State must lay before Parliament a copy of each such report
and certified statement.

34.2.2D

As soon as possible after the Secretary of State lays copies of the report and
statement of accounts before Parliament, S4C must arrange for the report and
certified statement to be laid before Senedd Cymru.

34.2.2E

S4C must ensure that each S4C subsidiary undertaking appoints the Comptroller
and Auditor General as auditor, unless the S4C subsidiary undertaking requests
the Comptroller and Auditor General’s permission to appoint another person and
the Comptroller and Auditor General permits the appointment of that person as
auditor.

34.2.2F

The Comptroller and Auditor General may inspect the accounts of any S4C
subsidiary undertaking (regardless of who is appointed as auditor).

34.3

After paragraph 12(4) insert—

34.3.5

S4C must ensure that an S4C subsidiary undertaking, if told to do so by the
Secretary of State or any person authorised by the Secretary of State, grants
the Secretary of State or authorised person access to—

34.3.5.a

that undertaking’s accounts;

34.3.5.b

information and documents relating to that undertaking’s financial
transactions and commitments.

34.3.6

In this paragraph “ S4C subsidiary undertaking ” means an undertaking which,
for the purposes of the Companies Act 2006, is a subsidiary undertaking of S4C
(see section 1162 of that Act).

34.4

Omit paragraph 13(2) (accounts and audit report to be attached to annual
report).

##### Amendment of BBC’s obligation to provide Welsh programmes

35

35.1

Section 58 of the Broadcasting Act 1990 (sources of programmes for S4C) is
amended as follows.

35.2

For subsections (1) and (1A) substitute—

35.2.1

The BBC must provide to S4C (free of charge) sufficient television programmes
in Welsh to occupy not less than ten hours’ transmission time per week, in a
way that meets the reasonable requirements of S4C.

35.2.1A

The duty in  subsection (1)  does not apply during any period for which the
BBC and S4C agree in writing to put in place alternative arrangements that
contribute to S4C fulfilling its public service remit.

35.2.1B

If the BBC and S4C make an agreement under  subsection (1A)  the BBC must, as
soon as reasonably practicable, publish the terms of the agreement.

35.2.1C

The BBC must exclude from publication any information which it or S4C
considers—

35.2.1C.a

constitutes a trade secret, or

35.2.1C.b

would be likely, if published, to prejudice the commercial interests of any
person,

unless the BBC and S4C consider that there is an overriding public interest in
publishing the information.

35.3

Omit subsections (2) to (4) (which relate to S4C’s switched-off analogue
service).

35.4

In subsection (5)—

35.4.a

for “The Welsh Authority” substitute  “S4C” ;

35.4.b

for “on S4C” substitute  “on S4C Digital” .

### On-demand programme services

#### Tier 1 services

37

37.1

Part 4A of the Communications Act 2003 (on-demand programme services) is
amended as follows.

37.2

After the heading of Part 4A insert—

  Chapter 1

  Introductory Provisions

.

37.3

After section 368A insert—

########## Meaning of non-UK on-demand programme service

37.3.368AA

37.3.368AA.1

For the purposes of this Act, a service (or a dissociable section of a
service) is a “non-UK on-demand programme service” if—

37.3.368AA.1.a

it meets the conditions in paragraphs (a) to (d) of section 368A(1),

37.3.368AA.1.b

it does not meet one or both of the conditions in paragraphs (e) and (f) of
section 368A(1), and

37.3.368AA.1.c

the members of the public for whose use it is made available are or include
members of the public in the United Kingdom.

37.3.368AA.2

Section 368A(5) to (7) applies in relation to a non-UK on-demand programme
service as it applies in relation to an on-demand programme service.

########## Overview of Part 4A

37.3.368AB

37.3.368AB.1

This section provides an overview of this Part.

37.3.368AB.2

This Chapter (Chapter 1) gives the meaning of certain expressions used in this
Part.

37.3.368AB.3

Chapter 2 contains provision for the regulation of on-demand programme
services (as defined by section 368A).

37.3.368AB.4

Chapter 3—

37.3.368AB.4.a

sets out the rules that apply for determining when an on-demand programme
service (as defined by section 368A) or a non-UK on-demand programme service
(as defined by  section 368AA ) is a Tier 1 service,

37.3.368AB.4.b

makes provision for certain sections of Chapter 2 to apply in relation to a
non-UK on-demand programme service that is a Tier 1 service in the same way
that they apply in relation to an on-demand programme service, and

37.3.368AB.4.c

makes provision for the additional regulation of Tier 1 services (whether on-
demand programme services or non-UK on-demand programme services).

37.3.368AB.5

Chapter 4 makes provision about the enforcement of certain provisions of
Chapters 2 and 3.

37.3.368AB.6

Chapter 5 makes supplementary provision.

37.4

In section 368B (the appropriate regulatory authority)—

37.4.a

after subsection (A1) insert—

37.4.a.A2

OFCOM is the appropriate regulatory authority for the purposes of sections
368HC ,  368HJ  and  368HK  (and OFCOM may not designate any other body to be
the appropriate regulatory authority for those purposes).

;

37.4.b

in subsection (1), after “subsections (A1)” insert  “, (A2)” ;

37.4.c

in subsection (5), in paragraph (a), after “on-demand programme services”
insert  “, or non-UK on-demand programme services that are Tier 1 services,” ;

37.4.d

in subsection (9), in paragraph (d), after “on-demand programme services”
insert  “or non-UK on-demand programme services” .

37.5

After section 368B insert—

  Chapter 2

  Regulation of on-demand programme services

.

37.6

After section 368H, insert (as Chapter 3 of Part 4A) the Chapter set out in
Schedule 5  (regulation of Tier 1 services).

37.7

Schedule 6  contains further amendments of Part 4A in connection with Tier 1
services (within the meaning of that Part).

37.8

Schedule 7  contains amendments of other legislation in connection with Tier 1
services (within the meaning of Part 4A of the Communications Act 2003).

#### Audience protection reviews

38

38.1

In Part 4A of the Communications Act 2003, after section 368OA insert—

########## Audience protection reviews etc

########### Audience protection reviews etc

38.1.368OB

38.1.368OB.1

As soon as practicable after this section comes into force, OFCOM must carry
out a review of audience protection measures in use by providers of—

38.1.368OB.1.a

on-demand programme services, or

38.1.368OB.1.b

non-UK on-demand programme services that are Tier 1 services.

38.1.368OB.2

The scope of that review is to consider whether the audience protection
measures are adequate for the purpose of assisting the providers to comply
with the duties imposed on them by or under this Act for the protection of
audiences from harm.

38.1.368OB.3

After the review under  subsection (1) , OFCOM may carry out further reviews
for the same purpose at such times as appear appropriate to OFCOM.

38.1.368OB.4

“Audience protection measures” are measures that are capable of assisting in
protecting audiences from harm, the following being examples—

38.1.368OB.4.a

age rating or other classification systems;

38.1.368OB.4.b

content warnings;

38.1.368OB.4.c

parental controls;

38.1.368OB.4.d

age assurance measures.

38.1.368OB.5

OFCOM may request any provider described in  subsection (1)  to provide OFCOM
with information about its audience protection measures for the purposes of a
review under  subsection (1)  or  (3) .

38.1.368OB.6

OFCOM may also request any provider described in  subsection (1)  to provide
OFCOM with information about its audience protection measures where, in
consequence of a review or anything else done in the exercise of their
functions, they are concerned that the measures in use by that provider are or
might be inadequate.

38.1.368OB.7

A request under  subsection (5)  or  (6)  must specify or describe the
information to be provided and may also—

38.1.368OB.7.a

specify a period of time within which the information must be provided;

38.1.368OB.7.b

specify the form and manner in which the information must be provided.

38.1.368OB.8

A request under  subsection (6)  may specify that information is to be
provided at intervals specified by OFCOM.

38.1.368OB.9

A provider described in  subsection (1)  must comply with a request under
subsection (5)  or  (6) .

38.1.368OB.10

OFCOM may publish any information provided to them under this section.

38.2

In section 393 of that Act (general restrictions on disclosure of
information), in subsection (6), after paragraph (aa) insert—

38.2.ab

limits the information that may be published by OFCOM under  section 368OB ;

.

#### Licensing and local services

42

42.1

The Broadcasting Act 1990 is amended as follows.

42.2

For section 104 (applications for other licences) substitute—

########## Applications for licences: local services and restricted services

42.2.104

42.2.104.1

An application for a licence to provide a local service must—

42.2.104.1.a

be made in such manner as OFCOM may determine, and

42.2.104.1.b

be accompanied by such fee (if any) as OFCOM may determine.

42.2.104.2

An application for a licence to provide a restricted service must—

42.2.104.2.a

be made in such manner as OFCOM may determine, and

42.2.104.2.b

be accompanied by such fee (if any) as OFCOM may determine.

42.3

In section 104AA (further renewal of local licences)—

42.3.a

in subsection (3), for “subsections (4), (4A) and (5)” substitute
“subsections (4) to (5)” ;

42.3.b

after subsection (4) insert—

42.3.b.4ZA

Where the application for the renewal of the licence under this section has
been duly made to OFCOM (as mentioned in section 104A(5)), OFCOM must grant
the application if—

42.3.b.4ZA.a

the condition in section 104A(5)(a) is met,

42.3.b.4ZA.b

the conditions in section 104A(5)(b) and (c) are not met because the applicant
does not make the nomination required by section 104A(4), and

42.3.b.4ZA.c

the alternative condition in  subsection (4ZB)  below is met instead.

42.3.b.4ZB

The alternative condition is met if—

42.3.b.4ZB.a

in the application for the renewal, or at any time before the consideration of
that application, the applicant makes to OFCOM—

42.3.b.4ZB.a.i

a statement of explanation — which is a statement that it has not been
possible for the applicant to make the nomination required by section 104A(4)
because of the lack of availability of a relevant local radio multiplex
service, or of a relevant small-scale radio multiplex service, that is
suitable for the applicant’s needs and could be nominated in accordance with
section 104A(4)(b); and

42.3.b.4ZB.a.ii

a statement of intent — which is a statement that the applicant will make to
OFCOM a nomination of the kind required by section 104A(4) as soon as it is
reasonably possible to do so because of the availability of a relevant local
radio multiplex service, or of a relevant small-scale radio multiplex service,
that is suitable for the applicant’s needs and meets the requirements of
section 104A(4); and

42.3.b.4ZB.b

OFCOM are satisfied that it has not been possible for the applicant to make
the nomination required by section 104A(4) for a reason of the kind set out in
paragraph  (a) (i) .

42.3.b.4ZC

Where OFCOM grant the application in accordance with  subsection (4ZA)  they
must include in the licence as renewed—

42.3.b.4ZC.a

a condition requiring the licence holder to do all that it can to ensure that
it makes the nomination described in the statement of intent as soon as it is
reasonably possible to do so, and

42.3.b.4ZC.b

a condition requiring the licence holder to do all that it can to ensure that
it starts broadcasting the nominated digital sound programme service, by means
of the nominated multiplex service, as soon as reasonably possible after it
has made that nomination.

42.4

Omit sections 104B (special application procedure for local licences) and 105
(special requirements relating to grant of local licences).

#### Local news and information

44

44.1

The Communications Act 2003 is amended in accordance with this section.

44.2

Section 314 (local content and character of local sound broadcasting services)
is amended in accordance with subsections (3) to (8).

44.3

For the heading substitute  “Local news and information in local sound
broadcasting services” .

44.4

For subsection (1) substitute—

44.4.1

A local sound broadcasting licence must contain such conditions as OFCOM
consider appropriate for—

44.4.1.a

requiring the licensed local sound broadcasting service to include, and
regularly broadcast, programmes that consist of or include local news and
information, and

44.4.1.b

requiring that local news to consist of or include locally-gathered news.

44.5

For subsection (1A) substitute—

44.5.1A

But subsection (1) does not apply in the case of a local sound broadcasting
service if OFCOM consider it is appropriate for it not to apply in that case.

44.6

In subsection (2)—

44.6.a

in paragraph (a), for “the requirements of subsection (1)(a) and (b) should be
satisfied” substitute  “the providers of local sound broadcasting services may
act consistently with conditions contained in licences in accordance with
subsection (1)” ;

44.6.b

in paragraph (b), for “in relation to local sound broadcasting services”
substitute  “under subsection (1)” .

44.7

In subsection (7)—

44.7.a

omit the definition of “approved area”;

44.7.b

in the definition of “local material”—

44.7.b.i

for ““local material”” substitute  ““local news and information”” ;

44.7.b.ii

for “means material” substitute  “means news and information” ;

44.7.c

for the definition of “locally-made” substitute—

      “ locally-gathered ”, in relation to news broadcast on a local sound
broadcasting service, means—         news gathered in the coverage area of a
local radio multiplex service that to a significant extent includes the
coverage area of the local sound broadcasting service by persons who gather
news in the course of an employment or business, or           if there is no
local radio multiplex service with such a coverage area, news gathered in the
area or locality for which the local sound broadcasting service is provided by
persons who gather news in the course of an employment or business;
and for this purpose the coverage area for a local radio multiplex service or
local sound broadcasting service is the area determined by OFCOM to be the
area in the United Kingdom within which the service is capable of being
received at a level satisfying such technical standards as may have been laid
down by them for the purposes of this section;

;

44.7.d

omit the definition of “material”.

44.8

Omit subsections (9) to (11).

44.9

After section 315 insert—

########## Local news and information in local digital radio services

44.9.315A

44.9.315A.1

The Secretary of State may, by regulations, make provision for enabling OFCOM
to ensure that, for each licensed local radio multiplex service, at least one
of the licensed local digital sound programme services broadcast by means of
that multiplex service consists of, or includes, local news and information or
locally-gathered news and information.

44.9.315A.2

The provision that may be made by regulations under this section includes
provision about the conditions that OFCOM may, or must, include in a licence
that authorises the provision of—

44.9.315A.2.a

a local digital sound programme service, or

44.9.315A.2.b

a local radio multiplex service.

44.9.315A.3

The Secretary of State must consult OFCOM before making regulations under this
section.

44.9.315A.4

The power in section 402(3)(c) for regulations under this section to make
consequential provision includes power to make provision which amends any
enactment.

44.9.315A.5

In this section—

      “ licensed ” local radio multiplex service or local digital sound
programme service means such a service which is provided in accordance with a
licence issued by OFCOM;           “ local news and information ”, in relation
to a local radio multiplex service or a local digital sound programme service
provided through such a multiplex service, means news and information which is
of particular interest—         to persons living or working within the area
or locality for which the multiplex service is provided;           to persons
living or working within a part of that area or locality; or           to
particular communities living or working within that area or locality or a
part of it;                 “ locally-gathered news ”, in relation to a local
radio multiplex service or a local digital sound programme service provided
through such a multiplex service, means news that has been gathered in the
area or locality for which the multiplex service is provided, by persons who
gather news in the course of an employment or business.

44.10

In section 402 (orders and regulations made by the Secretary of State), in
subsection (2A), before paragraph (za) (and after paragraph (zza) inserted by
section 46) insert—

44.10.zzb

regulations under section 315A which amend any Act of Parliament;

.

######## Financial assistance for radio

######### Power of the Secretary of State to give financial assistance for radio

45.359A

45.359A.1

The Secretary of State may give financial assistance for or in connection
with—

45.359A.1.a

the provision of eligible services;

45.359A.1.b

the production of sound programmes (whether intended for broadcast or
distribution by any other means).

45.359A.2

The financial assistance may be given—

45.359A.2.a

by way of grant, loan or guarantee or in any other form, and

45.359A.2.b

subject to such conditions as the Secretary of State considers appropriate.

45.359A.3

The conditions may (among other things) include provision under which the
financial assistance is to be repaid or otherwise made good (with or without
interest).

45.359A.4

45.359A.4.a

45.359A.4.b

local sound broadcasting services;

45.359A.4.c

local digital sound programme services.
