### Regulation of radio selection services

#### Regulation of radio selection services

48

48.1

After  section 362AZ12  of the Communications Act 2003 (inserted by  section
28 ) insert—

########## Regulation of radio selection services

########### Designated radio selection services

############ Meaning of “radio selection service”

48.1.362BA

48.1.362BA.1

In this Part, “ radio selection service ” means a service provided by means of
the internet which enables, or among other things enables, a user of the
service—

48.1.362BA.1.a

to make a selection between internet radio services provided by different
providers, and

48.1.362BA.1.b

to cause a selected internet radio service to play,

by giving spoken commands that are recorded by equipment connected to the
internet.

48.1.362BA.2

The Secretary of State may by regulations amend this section so as to alter
the definition of “radio selection service”.

48.1.362BA.3

The amendments that may be made by virtue of  subsection (2)  include—

48.1.362BA.3.a

amendments adding, removing or altering a thing that a radio selection service
is to enable a user to do, and

48.1.362BA.3.b

amendments adding, removing or altering a way in which a radio selection
service may be caused to operate.

48.1.362BA.4

The power in section 402(3)(c) for regulations under  subsection (2)  to make
consequential provision includes power to make provision which amends any
enactment.

48.1.362BA.5

Before making regulations under  subsection (2) , the Secretary of State must
consult OFCOM.

48.1.362BA.6

A statutory instrument containing regulations under  subsection (2)  may not
be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before and approved by
a resolution of each House of Parliament.

############ Meaning of “designated radio selection service”

48.1.362BB

48.1.362BB.1

For the purposes of this Part, a “designated radio selection service” is a
radio selection service designated by the Secretary of State by regulations.

48.1.362BB.2

The Secretary of State may designate a radio selection service under
subsection (1)  only if the Secretary of State considers that the level of use
of the service in the United Kingdom to listen to internet radio services is
significant (and the Secretary of State may consider the level of use to be
significant if the Secretary of State considers it to be significant in
certain circumstances, such as while in a vehicle).

48.1.362BB.3

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) , the Secretary of State must
have received a report under  section 362BC  relating to the radio selection
service in question.

48.1.362BB.4

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) , the Secretary of State must
consult—

48.1.362BB.4.a

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of radio
selection services;

48.1.362BB.4.b

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of
internet radio services;

48.1.362BB.4.c

such other persons as the Secretary of State considers appropriate.

48.1.362BB.5

The Secretary of State may by regulations amend this section so as to add or
remove a condition that must be satisfied before a radio selection service may
be designated under  subsection (1)  or to alter such a condition.

48.1.362BB.6

Subsection (4)  applies in relation to the making of regulations under
subsection (5)  as it applies in relation to the making of regulations under
subsection (1) .

48.1.362BB.7

The power in section 402(3)(c) for regulations under  subsection (5)  to make
consequential provision includes power to make provision which amends any
enactment.

48.1.362BB.8

A statutory instrument containing regulations under  subsection (5)  may not
be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before and approved by
a resolution of each House of Parliament.

############ Advice from OFCOM

48.1.362BC

48.1.362BC.1

OFCOM may prepare reports making recommendations about the exercise of the
power under  section 362BB (1) .

48.1.362BC.2

Where—

48.1.362BC.2.a

the Secretary of State proposes to make regulations under  section 362BB (1) ,
and

48.1.362BC.2.b

the Secretary of State has not received a report under  subsection (1)
relating to the radio selection service or services that would be affected by
the proposed regulations,

the Secretary of State must request OFCOM to prepare a report making
recommendations about exercising the power under  section 362BB (1)  in
relation to that service or those services.

48.1.362BC.3

Where the Secretary of State makes a request under  subsection (2) , OFCOM
must prepare such a report as soon as practicable.

48.1.362BC.4

A report under  subsection (1)  or  (3)  relating to the exercise of the power
under  section 362BB (1)  must include OFCOM’s assessment, in relation to each
radio selection service in question, of—

48.1.362BC.4.a

the number of members of the public using the service;

48.1.362BC.4.b

the manner in which the service is used by those persons;

48.1.362BC.4.c

whether the level of use of the service is significant;

48.1.362BC.4.d

such matters as OFCOM consider likely to affect the matters referred to in
paragraph (a) ,  (b)  or  (c) .

48.1.362BC.5

Where OFCOM prepares a report under  subsection (1)  or  (3) , OFCOM must—

48.1.362BC.5.a

give it to the Secretary of State, and

48.1.362BC.5.b

publish it.

48.1.362BC.6

If the Secretary of State exercises the power under  section 362BB (1)  in a
manner which differs from recommendations made in a report under this section,
the Secretary of State must publish, no later than the time at which the
regulations are made, a statement of the reasons for doing so.

48.1.362BC.7

OFCOM must draw up, and from time to time review and revise, a statement about
the principles and methods to be followed by OFCOM when preparing reports
under  subsection (1)  or  (3) .

48.1.362BC.8

OFCOM must publish the statement and any revised statement.

############ Revocation of designation of radio selection service

48.1.362BD

48.1.362BD.1

The Secretary of State may by regulations revoke the designation of a
designated radio selection service.

48.1.362BD.2

The provider of a designated radio selection service may request the Secretary
of State to revoke its designation.

48.1.362BD.3

The Secretary of State must revoke the designation of a designated radio
selection service by regulations under  subsection (1)  if the Secretary of
State considers that the level of use of the service in the United Kingdom to
listen to internet radio services is not significant.

48.1.362BD.4

Before revoking the designation of a designated radio selection service, the
Secretary of State must have received a report from OFCOM making
recommendations about the exercise of the power under  subsection (1)  in
relation to that service.

48.1.362BD.5

Where the Secretary of State requests OFCOM to prepare a report making
recommendations about the exercise of the power under  subsection (1)  in
relation to a designated radio selection service, OFCOM must—

48.1.362BD.5.a

prepare such a report in relation to that service as soon as practicable,

48.1.362BD.5.b

give it to the Secretary of State, and

48.1.362BD.5.c

publish it.

############ List of designated radio selection services etc

48.1.362BE

48.1.362BE.1

OFCOM must establish and maintain an up to date list of designated radio
selection services and their providers.

48.1.362BE.2

A provider of a designated radio selection service must give notice to OFCOM
if the service ceases to be provided.

48.1.362BE.3

A notice given to OFCOM under this section must—

48.1.362BE.3.a

be sent in such manner as OFCOM may require;

48.1.362BE.3.b

contain such information as OFCOM may require.

48.1.362BE.4

OFCOM must publish the list on a publicly accessible part of their website.

########### Relevant internet radio services

############ Meaning of “internet radio service”

48.1.362BF

48.1.362BF.1

In this Part, “ internet radio service ” means a service, or a dissociable
section of a service, which consists in the provision by a person of
programmes consisting wholly of sound (together with any ancillary services)
with a view to their being made available for reception by members of the
public by being distributed by means of the internet (whether by the provider
of the service or another person).

48.1.362BF.2

In this section, “ ancillary service ”, in relation to an internet radio
service, means a service which is provided by the provider of that internet
radio service and consists in the provision of a service (other than
advertising) which—

48.1.362BF.2.a

is ancillary to the programmes included in that internet radio service and is
directly related to their contents, or

48.1.362BF.2.b

relates to the promotion or listing of such programmes.

############ Meaning of “relevant internet radio service”

48.1.362BG

48.1.362BG.1

In this Part, “ relevant internet radio service ” means an internet radio
service for the time being included in the list maintained by OFCOM under
subsection (2) .

48.1.362BG.2

OFCOM must establish and maintain an up to date list of the internet radio
services in relation to which the conditions in subsections  (3)  and  (5)
are satisfied and their providers.

48.1.362BG.3

The condition in this subsection is that, in the opinion of OFCOM, the
provider of the service has in place an effective system or process for
securing that the service corresponds to a UK radio service that is provided
by the provider of the internet radio service.

48.1.362BG.4

For the purposes of subsection  (3) , an internet radio service corresponds to
a UK radio service if, disregarding advertisements, all of the programmes
included in the internet radio service are broadcast on the UK radio service
at the same time as they are provided by the internet radio service.

48.1.362BG.5

The condition in this subsection is that the provider of an internet radio
service—

48.1.362BG.5.a

has given notice to OFCOM requesting that the service be included in the list,
and

48.1.362BG.5.b

has not since then given notice to OFCOM under subsection  (6)  or  (7) .

48.1.362BG.6

The provider of an internet radio service included in the list may give notice
to OFCOM requesting that the service be removed from the list.

48.1.362BG.7

The provider of an internet radio service included in the list must give
notice to OFCOM if—

48.1.362BG.7.a

that person ceases to be the provider of the service,

48.1.362BG.7.b

that person ceases to be the provider of the UK radio service to which it
relates, or

48.1.362BG.7.c

the service ceases to be provided.

48.1.362BG.8

A notice given to OFCOM under this section must—

48.1.362BG.8.a

be sent in such manner as OFCOM may require;

48.1.362BG.8.b

contain such information as OFCOM may require.

48.1.362BG.9

OFCOM must take appropriate steps to keep the list up to date, including by
carrying out further assessments of whether a provider of an internet radio
service has in place such system or process as is described in  subsection (3)
.

48.1.362BG.10

OFCOM must publish the list on a publicly accessible part of their website.

48.1.362BG.11

In this section—

      “ digital sound programme service ” has the same meaning as in Part 2 of
the 1996 Act (see section 40 of that Act);           “ restricted service ”
has the same meaning as in section 245;           “ short-duration restricted
service ” means a restricted service authorised to be provided by a licence
under Part 3 of the 1990 Act where the period specified in the licence as the
period for which the licence is in force is less than 12 months;           “
sound broadcasting service ” has the same meaning as in Part 3 of the 1990 Act
(see section 126 of that Act);           “ UK radio service ” means—         a
sound broadcasting service, other than a short-duration restricted service,
provided by the BBC or authorised to be provided by a licence under Part 3 of
the 1990 Act, or           a digital sound programme service provided by the
BBC or authorised to be provided by a licence under Part 2 of the 1996 Act.

############ Sections 

48.1.362BH

48.1.362BH.1

The Secretary of State may by regulations—

48.1.362BH.1.a

amend section  362BF  so as to alter the definition of “internet radio
service”;

48.1.362BH.1.b

amend section  362BG  so as to alter the definition of “relevant internet
radio service”.

48.1.362BH.2

The amendments that may be made by virtue of  subsection (1) (a)  include
amendments adding or removing a condition that must be satisfied in relation
to a service or altering such a condition.

48.1.362BH.3

The amendments that may be made by virtue of  subsection (1) (b)  include
amendments adding or removing a condition that must be satisfied in relation
to an internet radio service or altering such a condition.

48.1.362BH.4

The conditions for which provision may be made by virtue of  subsection (3)
include conditions preventing or restricting charging for allowing the
internet radio service in question to be played.

48.1.362BH.5

The power in section 402(3)(c) for regulations under  subsection (1)  to make
consequential provision includes power to make provision which amends any
enactment.

48.1.362BH.6

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) , the Secretary of State must
consult—

48.1.362BH.6.a

OFCOM,

48.1.362BH.6.b

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of radio
selection services,

48.1.362BH.6.c

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of
internet radio services, and

48.1.362BH.6.d

such other persons as the Secretary of State considers appropriate.

48.1.362BH.7

A statutory instrument containing regulations under  subsection (1)  may not
be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before and approved by
each House of Parliament.

########### Regulation of radio selection services

############ Access to relevant internet radio services

48.1.362BI

48.1.362BI.1

The provider of a designated radio selection service must take all reasonable
steps to secure that users of the service—

48.1.362BI.1.a

are able, within a reasonable period beginning with the inclusion of an
internet radio service in the list under  section 362BG —

48.1.362BI.1.a.i

to select that internet radio service, and

48.1.362BI.1.a.ii

to cause that service to play,

by giving spoken commands as described in  section 362BA (1) , and

48.1.362BI.1.b

are able to continue to do so while that internet radio service is included in
the list.

48.1.362BI.2

The provider of a designated radio selection service must take all reasonable
steps to secure that, where the service is used as described in  subsection
(1) —

48.1.362BI.2.a

no items are played before the selected service is caused to play, other than—

48.1.362BI.2.a.i

a brief identification of the selected service,

48.1.362BI.2.a.ii

if the service employs another service (or other services) provided by means
of the internet to cause the selected service to play, a brief identification
of that other service (or one of those other services), and

48.1.362BI.2.a.iii

if the provider of the selected service agrees, one or more advertisements,
and

48.1.362BI.2.b

the playing of the selected service is not interrupted.

This subsection is subject to  subsection (5) .

48.1.362BI.3

Subsection (4)  applies if the provider of a relevant internet radio service
requests the provider of a designated radio selection service to secure that
the service employs a particular method as regards that relevant internet
radio service when complying with  subsection (1)  (for example, a method that
involves the service employing another service provided by means of the
internet to cause that relevant internet radio service to play).

48.1.362BI.4

Where this subsection applies, the provider of the designated radio selection
service must take all reasonable steps to secure that, on an occasion when the
service is being used as described in  subsection (1)  in relation to that
relevant internet radio service, the service employs that method, subject to
subsection (5) .

48.1.362BI.5

Subsections  (2)  and  (4)  are not to be taken to require the provider of a
designated radio selection service to override the preferences of a user of
the service as to the way in which the service operates.

48.1.362BI.6

A provider of a designated radio selection service—

48.1.362BI.6.a

must not charge a provider of a relevant internet radio service for doing what
that provider of a designated radio selection service is required to do by
subsection  (1) ,  (2)  or  (4)  in relation to that relevant internet radio
service, and

48.1.362BI.6.b

must not enter into an agreement that provides for the payment by a provider
of a relevant internet radio service of charges, which would breach, or are
capable of breaching, the prohibition in  paragraph (a) .

############ Further provision about access to relevant internet radio services

48.1.362BJ

48.1.362BJ.1

The provider of a designated radio selection service must draw up a statement
about how the provider intends to comply with the duties and prohibition in
section 362BI .

48.1.362BJ.2

The provider must keep the statement under review and, if appropriate, revise
it.

48.1.362BJ.3

The provider must publish the statement and any revised statement.

############ Code of practice

48.1.362BK

48.1.362BK.1

OFCOM must issue a code of practice describing actions that OFCOM recommend
for the purpose of securing that the manner in which a designated radio
selection service operates complies with the duties and prohibition in
section 362BI .

48.1.362BK.2

OFCOM may—

48.1.362BK.2.a

revise a code of practice issued under this section and issue the code as
revised;

48.1.362BK.2.b

withdraw a code of practice issued under this section and issue a new code of
practice.

48.1.362BK.3

OFCOM must—

48.1.362BK.3.a

publish a code of practice issued under this section in such manner as they
consider appropriate;

48.1.362BK.3.b

keep a code of practice issued under this section under review.

48.1.362BK.4

If requested by the Secretary of State to review all or part of a code of
practice issued under this section, OFCOM must review the code or that part of
it.

48.1.362BK.5

The actions recommended in a code of practice issued under this section may
include—

48.1.362BK.5.a

actions relating to particular descriptions of designated radio selection
services;

48.1.362BK.5.b

actions relating to particular descriptions of relevant internet radio
services.

############ Effects of the code of practice

48.1.362BL

48.1.362BL.1

The provider of a designated radio selection service is to be treated as
complying with a duty or prohibition in  section 362BI  if the provider takes
the actions described in the code of practice which are recommended for the
purpose of complying with that duty or prohibition.

48.1.362BL.2

A failure by the provider of a designated radio selection service to act in
accordance with a provision of the code of practice does not of itself make
the provider liable to legal proceedings before a court or tribunal.

48.1.362BL.3

In any legal proceedings before a court or tribunal, the court or tribunal
must take into account a provision of the code of practice in determining any
question arising in the proceedings if—

48.1.362BL.3.a

the question relates to a time when the provision was in force, and

48.1.362BL.3.b

the provision appears to the court or tribunal to be relevant to the question.

48.1.362BL.4

OFCOM must take into account a provision of the code of practice in
determining any question arising in connection with the carrying out by them
of a relevant function if—

48.1.362BL.4.a

the question relates to a time when the provision was in force, and

48.1.362BL.4.b

the provision appears to OFCOM to be relevant to the question.

48.1.362BL.5

In this section, “ relevant function ” means a function conferred on OFCOM by
any of sections  362BR  to  362BW  (enforcement).

############ Issuing a code of practice

48.1.362BM

48.1.362BM.1

Before issuing a code of practice under  section 362BK , OFCOM—

48.1.362BM.1.a

must publish a draft of the code or (as the case may be) a draft of the
revisions of the existing code;

48.1.362BM.1.b

must consult the following about the draft—

48.1.362BM.1.b.i

the Secretary of State;

48.1.362BM.1.b.ii

persons who appear to OFCOM to represent providers of internet radio services;

48.1.362BM.1.b.iii

persons who appear to OFCOM to represent providers of radio selection
services;

48.1.362BM.1.b.iv

such other persons as OFCOM consider appropriate;

48.1.362BM.1.c

may make such alterations to the draft as OFCOM consider appropriate following
the consultation.

48.1.362BM.2

Subsection  (1)  does not apply in relation to revisions of the code of
practice if—

48.1.362BM.2.a

OFCOM give the Secretary of State a draft of the revisions of the existing
code, and

48.1.362BM.2.b

the Secretary of State agrees that it is not necessary for subsection  (1)  to
apply in relation to the revisions.

############ Complaints procedures

48.1.362BN

The provider of a designated radio selection service must establish and
maintain procedures for the handling and resolution of complaints made by
providers of relevant internet radio services that the provider is failing, or
has failed, to comply with a duty or prohibition in  section 362BI .

########### Modification of regulation of radio selection services

############ Power to modify regulation

48.1.362BO

48.1.362BO.1

The Secretary of State may by regulations amend this Part so as to add to the
duties and prohibitions imposed on providers of radio selection services or to
alter or remove such a duty or prohibition.

48.1.362BO.2

The provision that may be made by regulations under  subsection (1)  includes—

48.1.362BO.2.a

provision about enabling the use of a radio selection service to select and
cause to play any relevant internet radio service of a particular sort (for
example, a service characterised by the nature of its contents or the identity
of its provider);

48.1.362BO.2.b

provision about the terms and conditions that may be offered by the provider
of a radio selection service to the provider of a relevant internet radio
service for or in connection with the use of the service to access the
relevant internet radio service;

48.1.362BO.2.c

provision about the charges that may be imposed by the provider of a radio
selection service on the provider of a relevant internet radio service in
connection with the use of the service to access the relevant internet radio
service;

48.1.362BO.2.d

provision about the publication of information about such terms, conditions
and charges.

48.1.362BO.3

The power in section 402(3)(c) for regulations under  subsection (1)  to make
consequential provision includes power to make provision which amends any
enactment.

48.1.362BO.4

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) , the Secretary of State must
have received a report of a review under  section 362BP .

48.1.362BO.5

Before making regulations under  subsection (1) , the Secretary of State must
consult—

48.1.362BO.5.a

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of
internet radio services;

48.1.362BO.5.b

persons who appear to the Secretary of State to represent providers of radio
selection services;

48.1.362BO.5.c

such other persons as the Secretary of State considers appropriate.

48.1.362BO.6

A statutory instrument containing regulations under  subsection (1)  may not
be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before and approved by
each House of Parliament.

############ Review by OFCOM

48.1.362BP

48.1.362BP.1

OFCOM may prepare reports that review the adequacy of the regulation of radio
selection services by this Part.

48.1.362BP.2

Where—

48.1.362BP.2.a

the Secretary of State proposes to make regulations under  section 362BO (1) ,
and

48.1.362BP.2.b

the Secretary of State has not received a report under  subsection (1) ,

the Secretary of State must request OFCOM to prepare a report that reviews the
adequacy of the regulation of radio selection services by this Part.

48.1.362BP.3

Where the Secretary of State makes a request under  subsection (2) , OFCOM
must prepare such a report as soon as practicable.

48.1.362BP.4

OFCOM must give the Secretary of State a report prepared under  subsection (1)
or  (3) .

48.1.362BP.5

OFCOM must publish reports given to the Secretary of State under this section.

########### Power to require information

############ Power to require information

48.1.362BQ

48.1.362BQ.1

OFCOM may by notice (an “information notice”) require a person within
subsection (4)  to provide them with any information that they require for the
purpose of carrying out their functions under this Part.

48.1.362BQ.2

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  includes power to require a person
within  subsection (4)  to obtain or generate information.

48.1.362BQ.3

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  must be exercised in a way that is
proportionate to the use to which the information is to be put by OFCOM.

48.1.362BQ.4

The persons within this subsection are—

48.1.362BQ.4.a

a provider of a radio selection service;

48.1.362BQ.4.b

a provider of an internet radio service;

48.1.362BQ.4.c

a person who provides a relevant ancillary service in relation to a radio
selection service or an internet radio service;

48.1.362BQ.4.d

a person who was within any of paragraphs  (a)  to  (c)  at a time to which
the required information relates;

48.1.362BQ.4.e

a person who is not within any of paragraphs  (a)  to  (d)  but who appears to
OFCOM to have, or to be able to obtain or generate, information required by
them as mentioned in  subsection (1) .

48.1.362BQ.5

The information that OFCOM may require under  subsection (1)  includes, in
particular, information that they require for any one or more of the following
purposes—

48.1.362BQ.5.a

the purpose of preparing a report under  section 362BC  (advice from OFCOM
about the designation of a radio selection service);

48.1.362BQ.5.b

the purpose of preparing a report under  section 362BD  (advice from OFCOM
about revoking the designation of a radio selection service);

48.1.362BQ.5.c

the purpose of assessing compliance with  section 362BE (2)  (duty of
providers of radio selection services to notify OFCOM);

48.1.362BQ.5.d

the purpose of assessing whether a service is a relevant internet radio
service (see sections  362BF  and  362BG );

48.1.362BQ.5.e

the purpose of assessing compliance with  section 362BG (7)  (duty of
providers of certain services to notify OCFOM);

48.1.362BQ.5.f

the purpose of assessing compliance with a duty or prohibition under  section
362BI  or  362BJ  (access duties of providers of designated radio selection
services etc);

48.1.362BQ.5.g

the purpose of preparing or reviewing a code of practice under section 362BK
(code of practice relating to duties and prohibition under  section 362BI );

48.1.362BQ.5.h

the purpose of assessing compliance with the duty under  section 362BN  (duty
to establish and maintain complaints procedures);

48.1.362BQ.5.i

the purpose of preparing a report under  section 362BP  (reports reviewing
adequacy of the regulation of designated radio selection services by this
Part);

48.1.362BQ.5.j

the purpose of assessing compliance with any requirements imposed by a
confirmation decision under  section 362BS ;

48.1.362BQ.5.k

the purpose of determining the appropriate fee that a provider is required to
pay under  section 362BX ;

48.1.362BQ.5.l

the purpose of OFCOM’s monitoring role under  section 362BZ1 ;

48.1.362BQ.5.m

the purpose of ascertaining the amount of a person’s or a group of entities’
qualifying worldwide revenue for the purposes of paragraph  3  or  4  of
Schedule 16A .

48.1.362BQ.6

An information notice must—

48.1.362BQ.6.a

specify or describe the information to be provided,

48.1.362BQ.6.b

specify why OFCOM require the information,

48.1.362BQ.6.c

specify the form and manner in which the information must be provided, and

48.1.362BQ.6.d

contain information about the consequences of not complying with the notice.

48.1.362BQ.7

An information notice must specify when the information must be provided which
may be—

48.1.362BQ.7.a

on or by a specified date, or

48.1.362BQ.7.b

within a specified period.

48.1.362BQ.8

The power conferred by  subsection (1)  does not include power to require the
provision of information in respect of which a claim to legal professional
privilege, or (in Scotland) to confidentiality of communications, could be
maintained in legal proceedings.

48.1.362BQ.9

A person to whom an information notice is given must provide the information
in accordance with any requirements included in the notice (subject to
subsection (10) ).

48.1.362BQ.10

The duty under  subsection (9)  does not require a disclosure of information
if that disclosure would contravene the data protection legislation (but, in
determining whether a disclosure would do so, that duty is to be taken into
account).

48.1.362BQ.11

For the purposes of  subsection (4) (c) , a service is a “ relevant ancillary
service ” in relation to a radio selection service or an internet radio
service if it facilitates the provision of that service (or part of it),
whether directly or indirectly.

48.1.362BQ.12

In this section, a reference to the functions of OFCOM under this Part
includes a reference to their functions under  Schedules 16A  and  16B , so
far as relating to this Part.

48.1.362BQ.13

In this section, “ data protection legislation ” has the same meaning as in
the Data Protection Act 2018 (see section 3 of that Act).

########### Enforcement

############ Provisional notices of contravention

48.1.362BR

48.1.362BR.1

OFCOM may give a notice under this section (a “provisional notice of
contravention”) to a person if they consider that there are reasonable grounds
for believing that the person has failed, or is failing, to comply with any
duty or prohibition under section  362BE ,  362BG ,  362BI ,  362BJ  or  362BN
.

48.1.362BR.2

OFCOM may also give a provisional notice of contravention to a person to whom
an information notice has been given if they consider that there are
reasonable grounds for believing that the person has failed, or is failing, to
comply with the duty under  section 362BQ (9) .

48.1.362BR.3

A provisional notice of contravention must—

48.1.362BR.3.a

specify the duty or prohibition as regards which (in OFCOM’s opinion) there
are reasonable grounds for believing the person has failed, or is failing, to
comply, and

48.1.362BR.3.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for that opinion.

48.1.362BR.4

A provisional notice of contravention may also specify steps that OFCOM
consider the person needs to take in order to—

48.1.362BR.4.a

comply with the duty or prohibition, or

48.1.362BR.4.b

remedy the failure to comply with it.

48.1.362BR.5

A provisional notice of contravention may also state that OFCOM propose to
impose a penalty on the person and, in such a case, the notice must—

48.1.362BR.5.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for proposing to impose the penalty,

48.1.362BR.5.b

indicate the amount in sterling of the proposed penalty, and

48.1.362BR.5.c

give OFCOM’s reasons for proposing a penalty of that amount, including any
aggravating or mitigating factors that OFCOM propose to take into account.

48.1.362BR.6

A provisional notice of contravention must—

48.1.362BR.6.a

state that the person may make representations to OFCOM (with any supporting
evidence) about the matters contained in the notice, and

48.1.362BR.6.b

specify the period within which such representations may be made.

48.1.362BR.7

A provisional notice of contravention may be given in respect of a failure by
the same person to comply with more than one duty or prohibition and, in such
a case, the notice may include a proposal to impose a single penalty in
respect of some or all of those duties or duties and prohibition (as an
alternative to separate penalties).

48.1.362BR.8

Where a provisional notice of contravention is given in respect of a
continuing failure to comply with a duty or prohibition, the notice—

48.1.362BR.8.a

may be given in respect of any period during which the failure has continued,

48.1.362BR.8.b

must specify that period, and

48.1.362BR.8.c

may include a proposal to impose no more than one penalty in respect of that
period.

48.1.362BR.9

Where a provisional notice of contravention is given to a person in respect of
a failure to comply with a duty or prohibition, a further provisional notice
of contravention in respect of a failure to comply with that same duty or
prohibition may be given to that person only—

48.1.362BR.9.a

in respect of a separate instance of the failure that occurs after the first
notice is given,

48.1.362BR.9.b

where a period is specified in the first notice in accordance with  subsection
(8) (b) , in respect of the continuation of the failure after the end of that
period, or

48.1.362BR.9.c

if the notice is withdrawn without a confirmation decision under  section
362BS  having been given to the person in respect of that failure.

48.1.362BR.10

OFCOM may give a provisional notice of contravention to—

48.1.362BR.10.a

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a designated radio selection
service, or

48.1.362BR.10.b

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a relevant internet radio
service,

if that person was a provider of a designated radio selection service or (as
the case may be) a relevant internet radio service at the time of the failure
to which the notice relates.

############ Confirmation decisions: general

48.1.362BS

48.1.362BS.1

This section applies where—

48.1.362BS.1.a

OFCOM have given a provisional notice of contravention to a person in relation
to a failure to comply with a duty or duties or a prohibition, and

48.1.362BS.1.b

the period allowed for representations has expired.

48.1.362BS.2

After considering any representations that have been made (and any supporting
evidence), OFCOM must decide whether or not to give the person a further
notice under this section (a “confirmation decision”).

48.1.362BS.3

OFCOM may decide to give a person a confirmation decision only if they are
satisfied that the person has failed, or has been failing, to comply with the
notified duty or one or more of the notified duties.

48.1.362BS.4

For the purposes of this section and sections  362BT  and  362BU , a “
notified duty ” means a duty or prohibition specified in the provisional
notice of contravention.

48.1.362BS.5

If OFCOM decide not to give a person a confirmation decision (whether because
they are not satisfied as described in  subsection (3)  or for any other
reason), they must inform the person of that fact.

48.1.362BS.6

A confirmation decision must—

48.1.362BS.6.a

state that OFCOM are satisfied that the person has failed, or has been
failing, to comply with one or more notified duties, and

48.1.362BS.6.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for being satisfied as described in  paragraph (a) .

48.1.362BS.7

A confirmation decision may require the person to take such steps as OFCOM
consider appropriate for either or both of the following purposes—

48.1.362BS.7.a

complying with a notified duty or duties;

48.1.362BS.7.b

remedying the failure to comply with that duty or those duties.

48.1.362BS.8

Where a provisional notice of contravention stated that OFCOM proposed to
impose a penalty in relation to a notified duty or (by virtue of  section
362BR (7) ) in relation to notified duties, a confirmation decision may
require the person to pay a penalty, of an amount in sterling determined by
OFCOM, in relation to that duty or (as the case may be) those duties.

48.1.362BS.9

The amount determined by OFCOM under  subsection (8)  may be greater than the
amount indicated in the provisional notice of contravention in accordance with
section 362BR (5) (b) .

48.1.362BS.10

OFCOM may give a confirmation decision to—

48.1.362BS.10.a

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a designated radio selection
service, or

48.1.362BS.10.b

a person who was but is no longer a provider of a relevant internet radio
service,

if that person was a provider of a designated radio selection service or (as
the case may be) a relevant internet radio service at the time of the failure
to which the decision relates.

############ Confirmation decisions: steps

48.1.362BT

48.1.362BT.1

This section applies where a confirmation decision requires the person to whom
it is given to take steps as provided for by  section 362BS (7) .

48.1.362BT.2

The notice must—

48.1.362BT.2.a

specify the steps that are required and the notified duty or duties to which
each relates,

48.1.362BT.2.b

give OFCOM’s reasons for requiring those steps to be taken,

48.1.362BT.2.c

specify a reasonable period within which each of the steps specified in the
notice must be taken, and

48.1.362BT.2.d

contain information about the consequences of not taking the steps (including
information about further kinds of enforcement action that it would be open to
OFCOM to take).

48.1.362BT.3

Where a confirmation decision requires a person to take steps, the person to
whom the notice is given has a duty to take those steps.

48.1.362BT.4

The duty under  subsection (3)  is enforceable in civil proceedings by OFCOM—

48.1.362BT.4.a

for an injunction;

48.1.362BT.4.b

for specific performance of a statutory duty under section 45 of the Court of
Session Act 1988;

48.1.362BT.4.c

for any other appropriate remedy or relief.

############ Confirmation decisions: penalties

48.1.362BU

48.1.362BU.1

This section applies where a confirmation decision imposes one or more
penalties (see  section 362BS (8) ).

48.1.362BU.2

In relation to each penalty imposed, the notice must—

48.1.362BU.2.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

48.1.362BU.2.b

specify each notified duty to which the penalty relates,

48.1.362BU.2.c

give OFCOM’s reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating
or mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

48.1.362BU.2.d

specify a reasonable period within which the penalty must be paid, and

48.1.362BU.2.e

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the kinds of enforcement action that it would be
open to OFCOM to take).

48.1.362BU.3

The period specified under  subsection (2) (d)  for the payment of a penalty
must be at least 28 days beginning with the day on which the confirmation
decision is given.

48.1.362BU.4

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a confirmation decision.

############ Penalty for failure to comply with confirmation decision

48.1.362BV

48.1.362BV.1

This section applies where—

48.1.362BV.1.a

OFCOM have given a confirmation decision to a person,

48.1.362BV.1.b

the notice includes requirements to take steps (as provided for by  section
362BS (7) ), and

48.1.362BV.1.c

OFCOM are satisfied that the person has failed to comply with one or more of
those requirements.

48.1.362BV.2

OFCOM may give the person a penalty notice.

48.1.362BV.3

A “penalty notice” is a notice requiring a person to pay to OFCOM a penalty of
an amount in sterling determined by OFCOM.

48.1.362BV.4

Before giving the person a penalty notice, OFCOM must—

48.1.362BV.4.a

notify the person that they propose to give a penalty notice in respect of the
failure to comply with the confirmation decision, specifying the reasons for
their proposal and indicating the amount of the proposed penalty, and

48.1.362BV.4.b

give the person an opportunity to make representations to OFCOM (with any
supporting evidence) about their proposal.

48.1.362BV.5

A penalty notice must—

48.1.362BV.5.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

48.1.362BV.5.b

state the amount of the penalty,

48.1.362BV.5.c

state the reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating or
mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

48.1.362BV.5.d

specify the period within which the penalty must be paid, and

48.1.362BV.5.e

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the further kinds of enforcement action that it
would be open to OFCOM to take).

48.1.362BV.6

The period specified under  subsection (5) (d)  must be at least 28 days
beginning with the day on which the penalty notice is given.

48.1.362BV.7

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a penalty notice.

############ Enforcement: guidance

48.1.362BW

48.1.362BW.1

OFCOM must prepare and publish guidance about the exercise of their powers
under sections  362BR  to  362BV  and  Schedule 16B  (so far as relating to
this Part).

48.1.362BW.2

The guidance must include the factors that OFCOM will take into account in
deciding whether to exercise any of those powers.

48.1.362BW.3

OFCOM may revise or replace any guidance published under this section and,
where they do so, must publish the revised or replacement guidance.

48.1.362BW.4

Before preparing guidance under this section (or revising or replacing it),
OFCOM must consult—

48.1.362BW.4.a

the Secretary of State, and

48.1.362BW.4.b

such other persons as they consider appropriate.

48.1.362BW.5

Guidelines prepared by OFCOM under section 392 (amount of penalties) may, so
far as relating to penalties imposed by a confirmation decision under  section
362BS  or a penalty notice under  section 362BV , be included in the same
document as guidance under this section.

48.1.362BW.6

In exercising or deciding whether to exercise any of their powers under
sections  362BR  to  362BV  and  Schedule 16B  (so far as relating to this
Part), OFCOM must have regard to any guidance for the time being published
under this section.

########### Supplemental provisions of Part 3B

############ Fees

48.1.362BX

48.1.362BX.1

OFCOM may require any of the following persons to pay to OFCOM a fee of an
amount determined by OFCOM—

48.1.362BX.1.a

a provider of a relevant internet radio service;

48.1.362BX.1.b

a provider of a designated radio selection service.

48.1.362BX.2

The amount of a fee required under  subsection (1)  must be determined by
OFCOM in accordance with a statement of principles prepared and published by
them for the purpose of this section.

48.1.362BX.3

Those principles must be such as appear to OFCOM to be likely to secure the
following objectives—

48.1.362BX.3.a

that, on a year by year basis, the aggregate amount of the fees payable to
OFCOM under  subsection (1)  is sufficient to meet, but does not exceed, the
annual cost to OFCOM of carrying out their functions under this Part less an
appropriate amount to take into account costs that will be met by fees payable
by the BBC under section 198(4);

48.1.362BX.3.b

that the relationship between the aggregate amount of the fees and the cost to
OFCOM of carrying out the functions is transparent;

48.1.362BX.3.c

that any fee required is justifiable and proportionate having regard to the
circumstances of the person required to pay it.

48.1.362BX.4

As soon as reasonably practicable after the end of each financial year, OFCOM
must publish a statement of accounts setting out in respect of that year—

48.1.362BX.4.a

the aggregate amount of the fees payable under  subsection (1)  for that year
that have been received by OFCOM,

48.1.362BX.4.b

the aggregate amount of the fees payable under  subsection (1)  for that year
that remain outstanding and are likely to be paid or recovered, and

48.1.362BX.4.c

the costs to them of carrying out their functions under this Part less an
appropriate amount to take into account costs that have been or are to be met
by fees payable by the BBC under section 198(4).

48.1.362BX.5

Any deficit or surplus shown (after applying this subsection for all previous
years) by the statement of accounts is to be—

48.1.362BX.5.a

carried forward, and

48.1.362BX.5.b

taken into account in determining what is required to meet the objective
described in  subsection (3) (a)  in relation to the following year.

48.1.362BX.6

OFCOM may repay a person some or all of a fee paid under  subsection (1)  if,
in the case of a fee paid by the provider of a designated radio selection
service—

48.1.362BX.6.a

the Secretary of State has revoked the designation of a designated radio
selection service provided by that person at some time during the period to
which the fee relates, or

48.1.362BX.6.b

the person gives OFCOM a notice under  section 362BE (2)  in accordance with
section 362BE (3)  at some time during the period to which the fee relates.

48.1.362BX.7

For the purposes of this section, OFCOM’s costs of carrying out their
functions under this Part during a financial year include their costs of
preparing to carry out those functions during that year.

48.1.362BX.8

OFCOM—

48.1.362BX.8.a

may revise a statement of principles published by them, and

48.1.362BX.8.b

where they do so, must publish the statement as revised.

48.1.362BX.9

Before publishing a statement of principles or a revision of it, OFCOM must
consult such persons as they consider appropriate.

48.1.362BX.10

In this section, a reference to the functions of OFCOM under this Part
includes a reference to their functions under  Schedules 16A  and  16B , so
far as relating to this Part.

48.1.362BX.11

In this section, “ financial year ” means a period of 12 months ending on 31
March.

############ Non-payment of fee

48.1.362BY

48.1.362BY.1

This section applies if—

48.1.362BY.1.a

the provider of a relevant internet radio service or a designated radio
selection service is liable to pay a fee to OFCOM under  section 362BX , and

48.1.362BY.1.b

in OFCOM’s opinion, the provider has not paid the full amount of the fee that
the provider is liable to pay.

48.1.362BY.2

OFCOM may give the provider a notice under this subsection specifying—

48.1.362BY.2.a

the outstanding amount of the fee that OFCOM consider the provider is due to
pay to them under  section 362BX , and

48.1.362BY.2.b

the period within which the provider must pay it.

48.1.362BY.3

A notice under  subsection (2) —

48.1.362BY.3.a

may relate to fees required on different occasions;

48.1.362BY.3.b

may also state that OFCOM propose to impose a penalty on the provider.

48.1.362BY.4

The provider may make representations to OFCOM (with any supporting evidence)
about the matters contained in the notice.

48.1.362BY.5

Subsection (6)  applies if—

48.1.362BY.5.a

the notice under  subsection (2)  stated that OFCOM propose to impose a
penalty,

48.1.362BY.5.b

the period allowed for representations has expired, and

48.1.362BY.5.c

OFCOM are satisfied that an amount of the fee or fees is still due to them.

48.1.362BY.6

OFCOM may give the provider a penalty notice under this subsection requiring
the provider to pay to OFCOM a penalty of an amount in sterling determined by
OFCOM.

48.1.362BY.7

The penalty may consist of any of the following—

48.1.362BY.7.a

a single amount;

48.1.362BY.7.b

an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate;

48.1.362BY.7.c

a combination of a single amount and an amount calculated by reference to a
daily rate.

48.1.362BY.8

The penalty notice may impose a penalty of a different kind, of a greater
amount or (in the case of a penalty calculated by reference to a daily rate)
payable over a longer period than that proposed in the notice about the
proposed penalty.

48.1.362BY.9

See  section 362BZ  for information which must be included in notices under
this section.

48.1.362BY.10

Nothing in this section affects OFCOM’s power to bring proceedings (whether
before or after the imposition of a penalty by a notice under  subsection (6)
) for the recovery of the whole or part of an amount due to OFCOM under
section 362BX .

48.1.362BY.11

But OFCOM may not bring such proceedings unless a provider has first been
given a notice under  subsection (2)  specifying the amount due to OFCOM.

############ Information to be included in a notice under 

48.1.362BZ

48.1.362BZ.1

A notice under  section 362BY (2)  stating that OFCOM propose to impose a
penalty must—

48.1.362BZ.1.a

state the reasons why OFCOM propose to impose the penalty,

48.1.362BZ.1.b

state whether OFCOM propose that the penalty should consist of a single
amount, an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, or a combination of
the two,

48.1.362BZ.1.c

indicate the amount of the proposed penalty, including (in relation to an
amount calculated by reference to a daily rate) the daily rate and how the
penalty would be calculated,

48.1.362BZ.1.d

in relation to an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, specify or
describe the period for which OFCOM propose that the amount should be payable,

48.1.362BZ.1.e

state the reasons for proposing a penalty of that amount, including any
aggravating or mitigating factors that OFCOM propose to take into account, and

48.1.362BZ.1.f

specify the period within which representations in relation to the proposed
penalty may be made.

48.1.362BZ.2

A penalty notice under  section 362BY (6)  must—

48.1.362BZ.2.a

give OFCOM’s reasons for their decision to impose the penalty,

48.1.362BZ.2.b

state whether the penalty consists of a single amount, an amount calculated by
reference to a daily rate, or a combination of the two, and how it is
calculated,

48.1.362BZ.2.c

in relation to a single amount, state that amount,

48.1.362BZ.2.d

in relation to an amount calculated by reference to a daily rate, state the
daily rate,

48.1.362BZ.2.e

state the reasons for the amount of the penalty, including any aggravating or
mitigating factors that OFCOM have taken into account,

48.1.362BZ.2.f

specify a reasonable period within which the penalty must be paid, and

48.1.362BZ.2.g

contain information about the consequences of not paying the penalty
(including information about the further kinds of enforcement action that it
would be open to OFCOM to take).

48.1.362BZ.3

A penalty notice under  section 362BY (6)  must also specify the amount of the
fee that is (in OFCOM’s opinion) due to be paid to OFCOM.

48.1.362BZ.4

The period specified under  subsection (2) (f)  for the payment of a single
amount must be at least 28 days beginning with the day on which the penalty
notice is given.

48.1.362BZ.5

Subsection (6)  applies in relation to a penalty notice under  section 362BY
(6)  that includes a requirement to pay an amount calculated by reference to a
daily rate.

48.1.362BZ.6

Such a notice must—

48.1.362BZ.6.a

state the date from which the amount begins to be payable, which must not be
earlier than the day after the day on which the notice is given;

48.1.362BZ.6.b

provide for the amount to continue to be payable at the daily rate until—

48.1.362BZ.6.b.i

the date on which the full amount of the fee (as specified in the penalty
notice) has been paid to OFCOM, or

48.1.362BZ.6.b.ii

an earlier date specified in the penalty notice.

48.1.362BZ.7

Schedule 16A  contains further provision about the imposition of a penalty by
a penalty notice under  section 362BY (6) .

############ Monitoring role for OFCOM

48.1.362BZ1

OFCOM have the function of obtaining, compiling and keeping under review
information about matters which may be relevant to—

48.1.362BZ1.a

designating or revoking the designation of a radio selection service (see
sections  362BB  and  362BD );

48.1.362BZ1.b

deciding whether to take enforcement action under this Part and Schedule 16B
(so far as relating to this Part).

############ Notices

48.1.362BZ2

48.1.362BZ2.1

This section applies in relation to a notice that may or must be given by
OFCOM to a person under any provision of this Part or Schedule 16B (so far as
relating to this Part).

48.1.362BZ2.2

OFCOM may give a notice to a person by—

48.1.362BZ2.2.a

delivering it by hand to the person,

48.1.362BZ2.2.b

leaving it at the person’s proper address,

48.1.362BZ2.2.c

sending it by post to the person at that address, or

48.1.362BZ2.2.d

sending it by email to that person’s email address.

48.1.362BZ2.3

A notice to a body corporate may be given to any officer of that body.

48.1.362BZ2.4

A notice to a partnership may be given to any partner or to a person who has
the control or management of the partnership business.

48.1.362BZ2.5

A notice to an entity that is not a legal person under the law under which it
is formed (other than a partnership) may be given to any member of the
governing body of the entity.

48.1.362BZ2.6

In the case of a notice given to a person who is a provider of a designated
radio selection service, the person’s proper address for the purposes of
paragraphs  (b)  and  (c)  of  subsection (2) , and section 7 of the
Interpretation Act 1978 in its application to those paragraphs, is any address
(within or outside the United Kingdom) at which OFCOM believe, on reasonable
grounds, that the notice will come to the attention of the person or (where
that person is an entity) any director or other officer of that entity.

48.1.362BZ2.7

In the case of a notice given to a person other than a provider of a
designated radio selection service, a person’s proper address for the purposes
of paragraphs  (b)  and  (c)  of  subsection (2) , and section 7 of the
Interpretation Act 1978 in its application to those paragraphs, is—

48.1.362BZ2.7.a

in the case of an entity, the address of the entity’s registered or principal
office;

48.1.362BZ2.7.b

in any other case, the person’s last known address.

48.1.362BZ2.8

In the case of an entity registered or carrying on business outside the United
Kingdom, or with offices outside the United Kingdom, the reference in
subsection (7)  to its principal office includes—

48.1.362BZ2.8.a

its principal office in the United Kingdom, or

48.1.362BZ2.8.b

if the entity has no office in the United Kingdom, any place in the United
Kingdom at which OFCOM believe, on reasonable grounds, that the notice will
come to the attention of any director or other officer of that entity.

48.1.362BZ2.9

For the purposes of  subsection (2) (d) , a person’s email address is—

48.1.362BZ2.9.a

any email address published for the time being by that person as an address
for contacting that person, or

48.1.362BZ2.9.b

if there is no such published address, any email address by means of which
OFCOM believe, on reasonable grounds, that the notice will come to the
attention of that person or (where that person is an entity) any director or
other officer of that entity.

48.1.362BZ2.10

A notice sent by email is treated as given 48 hours after it was sent, unless
the contrary is proved.

48.1.362BZ2.11

In this section—

      “ director ” includes any person occupying the position of a director,
by whatever name called;           “ officer ”, in relation to an entity,
includes a director, a manager, a partner, an associate, a secretary or, where
the affairs of the entity are managed by its members, a member.

############ Application of Part 3B

48.1.362BZ3

48.1.362BZ3.1

A duty or prohibition imposed on a provider of a designated radio selection
service by or under this Part applies in relation to that service only so far
as it is made available for use by members of the public in the United
Kingdom.

48.1.362BZ3.2

References in this Part to a radio selection service include such a service
provided from outside the United Kingdom (as well as such a service provided
from within the United Kingdom).

48.1.362BZ3.3

The power to require the provision of information by an information notice
includes power to require the provision of information held outside the United
Kingdom.

48.1.362BZ3.4

Section  362BT (4)  (requirements enforceable in civil proceedings against a
person) applies whether or not the person is in the United Kingdom.

############ Interpretation of Part 3B

48.1.362BZ4

48.1.362BZ4.1

In this Part—

      “ ancillary service ”, in relation to an internet radio service, has the
meaning given by  section 362BF  (except in the expression “ relevant
ancillary service ”);           “ designated radio selection service ” has the
meaning given by  section 362BB ;           “ entity ” means a body or
association of persons or an organisation, regardless of whether the body,
association or organisation is—         formed under the law of any part of
the United Kingdom or of a country or territory outside the United Kingdom, or
a legal person under the law under which it is formed;                 “
information notice ” has the meaning given by  section 362BQ ;           “
internet radio service ” has the meaning given by  section 362BF ;           “
provide ”, in relation to a sound broadcasting service or digital sound
programme service, has the same meaning as in Part 3 (see section 362(2) and
(3));           “ radio selection service ” has the meaning given by  section
362BA ;           “ relevant internet radio service ” has the meaning given by
section 362BG .

48.1.362BZ4.2

A reference in this Part to the playing of an internet radio service includes
a reference to providing its ancillary services (if any).

48.2

Schedule 9  contains further amendments relating to regulation of radio
selection services.

#### Amendments related to the UK's withdrawal from the EU

##### Amendments of broadcasting legislation: UK’s withdrawal from EU

51

Schedule 12  contains amendments of the Broadcasting Act 1990, the
Broadcasting Act 1996 and the Communications Act 2003 to address failures of
retained EU law to operate effectively and other deficiencies arising from the
withdrawal of the United Kingdom from the European Union.

#### General

##### Power to make consequential provision

52

52.1

The Secretary of State may by regulations make provision that is consequential
on this Act.

52.2

Regulations under this section may amend, repeal or revoke provision made by
or under an Act passed—

52.2.a

before this Act, or

52.2.b

in the same session of Parliament as this Act.

52.3

Regulations under this section may—

52.3.a

make different provision for different purposes;

52.3.b

make transitional, transitory or saving provision.

52.4

Regulations under this section are to be made by statutory instrument.

52.5

A statutory instrument containing (whether alone or with other provision)
regulations under this section that amend or repeal any provision of an Act
may not be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before, and
approved by a resolution of, each House of Parliament.

52.6

Any other statutory instrument containing regulations under this section is
subject to annulment in pursuance of a resolution of either House of
Parliament.

##### Financial provisions

53

There is to be paid out of money provided by Parliament any increase
attributable to the Act in the sums payable under any other Act out of money
so provided.

##### Extent

54

54.1

This Act extends to England and Wales, Scotland and Northern Ireland, subject
to  subsection (2) .

54.2

An amendment or repeal made by this Act has the same extent within the United
Kingdom as the provision amended or repealed.

54.3

The power under—

54.3.a

section 204(6) of the Broadcasting Act 1990,

54.3.b

section 150(4) of the Broadcasting Act 1996, or

54.3.c

section 411(6) of the Communications Act 2003,

may be exercised so as to extend to any of the Channel Islands or the Isle of
Man any amendment or repeal made by or under this Act of any part of the
Broadcasting Act 1990, the Broadcasting Act 1996 or the Communications Act
2003 (with or without modifications).

54.4

His Majesty may by Order in Council provide for any of the other provisions of
this Act to extend, with or without modifications, to any of the Channel
Islands or to the Isle of Man.

##### Commencement

55

55.1

The following come into force on the day on which this Act is passed—

55.1.a

Part 2 , so far as it confers powers to make regulations;

55.1.b

sections  52  to  54 , this section and  section 56 .

55.2

Section  50  comes into force at the end of the period of two months beginning
with the day on which this Act is passed.

55.3

The following come into force on such day as the Secretary of State may by
regulations appoint—

55.3.a

Part 1 ;

55.3.b

the remaining provisions of  Part 2 ;

55.3.c

Part 3 ;

55.3.d

Part 4 ;

55.3.e

Part 5 ;

55.3.f

Part 6 ;

55.3.g

section 49  and  Schedules 10  and  11 ;

55.3.h

section 51  and  Schedule 12 .

55.4

Different days may be appointed for different purposes.

55.5

The Secretary of State may by regulations make transitional, transitory or
saving provision in connection with the coming into force of any provision of
this Act.

55.6

The power to make regulations under  subsection (5)  includes power to make
different provision for different purposes.

55.7

Regulations under this section are to be made by statutory instrument.

##### Short title

56

This Act may be cited as the Media Act 2024.

If OFCOM—

16.2.A1.a

are satisfied that a person other than the BBC or S4C who is the provider of a
relevant service has failed to comply with section  101 (1) , and

16.2.A1.b

are not satisfied that in all the circumstances it would be unreasonable to
have expected the person to have complied with that provision,

they may require the person to pay, within a specified period, a specified
financial penalty to OFCOM.

16.2.B1

If OFCOM are satisfied that, in connection with an application for consent for
the purposes of section  101 (5) , a person other than the BBC or S4C who is
the provider of a relevant service has—

16.2.B1.a

provided them with information which was false in a material particular, or

16.2.B1.b

withheld any material information with the intention of causing OFCOM to be
misled,

they may require the person to pay, within a specified period, a specified
financial penalty to OFCOM.

16.3

In subsection (1)(a), omit “subsection (1) of section 101 or”.

16.4

in subsection (2), for “under subsection (1) of section 101 or” substitute
“for the purposes of” .

16.5

In subsection (3), after “subsection” insert  “ (A1) ,  (B1) ,” .

16.6

—

16.6.i

in relation to a financial penalty imposed under  subsection (A1)  or  (B1) ,
an amount determined by OFCOM to be the value of the rights to include
coverage of the event in question in the relevant service at the time when the
rights are acquired, and

16.6.ii

in relation to a financial penalty imposed under subsection (1) or (2),

.

19.7

After subsection (1) insert—

19.7.1A

The services that are to be taken for the purposes of this Part to be
available to members of the public include any service which—

19.7.1A.a

is available for reception by members of the public (within the meaning of
section 361 of the Communications Act 2003), or

19.7.1A.b

is available for use by members of the public (within the meaning of section
368R(4) of the Communications Act 2003).

19.7.1B

In this Part—

19.7.1B.a

a reference to the provision of a television programme service is to be read
in accordance with section 362(2) and (3) of the Communications Act 2003;

19.7.1B.b

a reference to the provision of an on-demand programme service or a non-UK on-
demand programme service is to be read in accordance with section 368R(5) and
(6) of the Communications Act 2003.

19.7.1C

In this Part, the person, and the only person, who is to be treated for the
purposes of this Part as providing a relevant service of the kind described in
section 98(7)(d) is the person who has such control of the service as is
described in section 98(7)(d)(iii).

19.7.1D

For the purposes of this Part as it relates to relevant services of the kind
described in section 98(7)(d)—

19.7.1D.a

the provision of a service by the BBC does not include its provision by a BBC
company;

19.7.1D.b

the provision of a service by S4C does not include its provision by an S4C
company;

and, accordingly, control that is capable of being exercised by the BBC or S4C
over decisions by a BBC company or an S4C company about what is to be included
in a service is to be disregarded for the purposes of determining who has such
control of the service as is described in section 98 (7) (d) (iii) .

##### Equality Act 2010
